European and American Aviation Competition 51

Reuter's, London, 21st - Participants in the European International Aviation Competition are being held up by thunderstorms and fog in Calais and Lyme, France.

Associated Press, New York, 20th - The first leg of the International Air Race will be held here tomorrow. The route is set at 7,500 miles, departing from New York, going to Atlanta in Huston, crossing the American border to Mexico City, and then returning via Dallas, El Paso, Los Angeles, Salt Lake City, Omaha, Chicago, Montreal, and back to New York. The one with the shortest time wins first place, with a prize of US$15,000, second place receives $7,000, and third place receives $3,000. More than 100 people have joined the competition, with no restrictions on gender or nationality, but they must hold a flight license from any government. There are also no restrictions on the type of aircraft used, whether manufactured in the United States or not, they can all participate. Each participant is free to stop at any location, but the duration of their stop cannot be deducted.

Reuter's, Berlin, 24th - Sixty fliers departed from the Danpelhof airfield today to participate in the European International Aviation Competition. The flight distance is 4,000 miles, passing through Belgium, France, England, Spain, Switzerland, Austria, Czechoslovakia, Poland, and then returning to Berlin. It will take twelve days. There are 27 monitoring stations along the way. When each aircraft flies out, its engine is sealed, and no important parts are allowed to be replaced. Seven British fliers are participating, including two women.

Important News

Memorial Week for the Central Government and the National Government 52

Central Party Headquarters: At 9:00 a.m. on the 21st, the Central Party Headquarters held the 69th Dr. Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week in the auditorium. Central Committee members Chen Guofu, Zeng Yangfu, Chen Lifu, Enkebatu Kexing'e, Yu Jingtang, etc., and officials from various departments and guests, totaling about 500 people, attended. Chen Guofu chaired the meeting. After the ceremony, Zeng Yangfu was asked to give a report, which stated that the so-called expanded conference in Peiping recently was asking what valid reason there was to give rise to this "expanded" name. The terms of office of the 1st and 2nd Central Committees had long expired. Even in terms of the number of members in the 2nd Committee, those serving the Party in Nanjing Central were greater than those who agreed with the reactionaries in Peiping. A comparison will easily make this clear. Furthermore, does the Party's general charter allow for the establishment of special organizations, and is there a possibility of expanding the scope? This is also self-evident. Examining its content, those listed as participating in this conference include Communists, quasi-Communists, opportunists, and corrupt elements. The participants are a mixture of all types, which can be described as a large group of counter-revolutionaries. Their purpose is to use warlords to maintain their personal status and rights, at the expense of violating Party discipline and disregarding Party authority. They claim to protect the Party and save the country, but in reality, they are destroying the Party and disrupting the country. They know that the warlords want to use reactionaries to destroy the Party, but they do not hesitate to flatter the warlords, to seek personal gain by selling out the Party. Dr. Sun said to seek peace and work hard to save China, but they insist on disrupting peace, preventing national unification, in order to achieve their separatist ambitions. Their rebellious actions are already obvious, yet they still boast of courtesy to deceive themselves and others. The eyes and ears of the people of the world cannot be covered up by one hand. I believe that the people of the whole country have full faith in the Nanjing Central Government and will not be deceived by their childish organization. Looking back at the causes and effects of the Party's history, there has never been a case where violating the ideology, losing public trust, and combining for the personal gain of a few people could last long. As long as the Party comrades can implement the spirit and work hard, this kind of boring act will soon be eliminated. As for the warlords Yan and Feng, who instigated rebellion, they promoted a kind of rhetoric, the so-called Northern Great Unity, to resist the Southern invaders, using this to bewitch the people of the North. The imperialists also used the slogan of North-South War to provoke mutual animosity and make unification never succeed. However, all Chinese people with a little common sense know that the Chinese nation has always been a whole, and does not recognize the division between North and South. Moreover, the Central Army's brave sacrifices on the front lines this time were mostly made by valiant soldiers from the North. The spirit of North-South cooperation to overthrow the warlords is clearly evident. Therefore, this war is a great battle between revolution and counter-revolution, and also the final movement to achieve peaceful unification. The Party comrades should strive to consolidate the foundation of the Party, always take the ideology as the standpoint, show a very excellent mindset, and not cause disputes due to minor incidents, nor harbor resentment due to accidental misunderstandings. With one heart and one mind, we should concentrate our inherent strength and carry out construction work, and constantly reflect on ourselves and remedy our shortcomings. Then the great success of the Party's ideology can be expected. The meeting was adjourned after the report.

National Government: At 10:00 a.m. on the same day, the National Government held Dr. Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week. Tan Yankai, Gu Yingfen, Yu Zhengting, Zhang Nanxian, Jiang Menglin, Lin Xiang, Zhu Lühe, Li Jinlun, Zhu Jingnong, Mu Xiangyue, Zhu Peide, Chen Yi, Zhou Yawei, Wu Siyu, Chen Yu, Ma Fuxiang, Zhang Wohua, Chen Shaokuan, Zheng Hongnian, and officials from the National Government's civil and military departments, totaling more than 200 people, attended. Tan Yankai chaired the meeting. Secretary Qian Changzhao gave the following political report: "At 2:00 p.m. on the 13th, the so-called expanded conference in Huiren Hall, Peiping, actually opened. Yan and Feng can combine, the Reorganization Faction and the Western Hills Faction can combine, and Yan, Feng, the Reorganization, and Western Hills Factions can also combine. Now the expanded conference of fifteen people has actually been established. It is truly absurd. This kind of conference has no basis in the Party and increases turmoil in the country. Furthermore, the psychology of the parties involved in the conference is even more despicable and sordid. Now, let's analyze them. Yan and Feng combine for the sake of interests, which is not surprising. Yan and Feng have long forgotten about the Party. This time, they suddenly combined with the Reorganization and Western Hills Factions, wanting nothing more than to take advantage of them. The initial purpose of taking advantage of them is twofold: (1) To collude with Zhang Gui's remnants and rebels. Yan and Feng's relationship with Zhang Gui's remnants and rebels is too shallow, relying entirely on people from the Reorganization and Western Hills Factions to run errands between them. (2) Yan and Feng are not very clear about the content of the Reorganization and Western Hills Factions, and still think that they have a large potential influence in the North and South, and that they can help to make trouble in the South, and to help with propaganda in the North. But who knew that they all failed? Although Zhang Gui's remnants and rebels once stirred up trouble, they were immediately defeated and completely annihilated by the Central Government, and cannot cause trouble. Even the troublemaking and propaganda of the Reorganization and Western Hills Factions in various places did not achieve any results. Therefore, Yan and Feng's anger became greater day by day, and the Reorganization and Western Hills Factions had to be especially accommodating. Now, let's first talk about Yan's attitude towards the Reorganization and Western Hills Factions. Since Yan's defection, he has been in a panic and at a loss. He wanted to contact all kinds of reactionaries to resist the Central Government. The Reorganization and Western Hills Factions had already been running errands for him before the defection, so after the defection, they were naturally "honored guests." Although the work of the Reorganization and Western Hills Factions has not been very successful recently, Yan feels that inviting them to Peiping has cost him a lot of money, so he always wants to use them again. At the same time, Yan knows that Feng is very difficult to get along with, and he is neither willing to be under Feng nor dare to take the lead over Feng, so he is brewing an expanded conference, ostensibly to do the work of urging him to advance. On the day the expanded conference opened, the conference's signature book was the Reorganization and Western Hills Factions' contract of sale. In the event that a puppet government is established, when urging them to advance in the future, they can calmly do a set of "firmly rejecting and reluctantly accepting the difficult task" with Feng, avoiding the suspicion of seizing power themselves. What is pitiful is that the Reorganization and Western Hills Factions are always being used. Tan Zhen and others have gone to Jin to "respectfully listen to instructions" (Tan Zhen's telegram to Yan contains this phrase), and Yan can "personally impart guidance." Let's talk about Feng's attitude towards the Reorganization and Western Hills Factions. Feng has always been able to use everything, but this time he seems to be somewhat contemptuous of the Reorganization and Western Hills Factions. We only need to look at the time when he used Christianity, he also prayed and read the Bible every day. When he used the Communist Party, he also personally went to Moscow and invited Xu Qian to live across from him, participating in secret matters. And this time, when using the Reorganization and Western Hills Factions, he only sent telegrams and had unimportant second- or third-rate roles (Feng's second- or third-rate roles) Huang Shaogu and others perfunctorily deal with them. As for the opening of the expanded conference and Yan's intentions, how could Feng not know? But in times of military tension, he is happy to let the Reorganization and Western Hills Factions encourage the establishment of a puppet government, to recommend Yan as chairman, and then the pay and ammunition of Feng's troops will also have a place to go. Yan and Feng's attitude towards the Reorganization and Western Hills Factions is like this. What about the Reorganization and Western Hills Factions themselves? They run errands for Yan and Feng, not to devote themselves to Yan and Feng, but in reality they are a group of frustrated politicians. Some are restless and greedy for wealth. Some were relatively law-abiding in the past, but this time they were fooled by others. Therefore, the two factions that were incompatible in the past actually combined, held a conference, issued a declaration, and supported Yan and Feng, acting as accomplices. They may know that Yan and Feng will eventually fail. They may know that relying on Yan and Feng for a living will not last long. It's just that they are too hungry to be picky, so they have to get by. In fact, there is now no so-called Reorganization Faction or so-called Western Hills Faction. These terms are meaningless. It would be better to simply call them the Expanded Faction. The expanded conference is a tool of the feudal warlords. It is a puppet show to seize power for others. From this, one can estimate the value of the middle members of the Expanded Faction. Speaking of this point, I can't help but feel infinitely emotional. Among the members of the Reorganization and Western Hills Factions, there are many people who have a considerable history with the revolution. If they had not gone astray, they could have contributed greatly to society and the country. Even if they had gone astray, if they could turn back in time, the Central Government would be willing to accept them. But unfortunately, they are lost and do not return. When the feudal warlords are making their last struggles and the Central Government is launching a punitive expedition against them, they actually go to great lengths to be sycophantic and sacrifice their many years of revolutionary history and personality. What a pity. The decline of the Reorganization and Western Hills Factions is probably irreversible. It is hoped that all revolutionary comrades will see their decline and encourage themselves more in the future, always unite and not allow any phenomenon of disintegration. Then, even if the revolutionary future is difficult, it will not be difficult to overcome, and the success of the revolution will be hopeful."

National Government Announces the Law on Election and Recall of Autonomous Officials 53

The Law on Election and Recall of Autonomous Officials of Townships, Towns, and Neighborhoods was promulgated by the National Government on the 21st. The full text is as follows:

Chapter I: General Provisions. (Article 1) The election and recall of autonomous officials of townships, towns, and neighborhoods shall be governed by the provisions of this Law, except as otherwise provided in the County Organization Law, the Township and Town Autonomy Implementation Law, and the City Organization Law. (Article 2) The term "autonomous officials" as used in this Law shall refer to the following officials: 1. The chief and deputy chief of a township, and the township supervisory committee members. 2. The chief and deputy chief of a town, and the town supervisory committee members. 3. The head of a neighborhood and the neighborhood supervisory committee members. (Article 3) The term "candidate" as used in this Law shall refer to a person who is legally qualified to be a candidate for any of the autonomous officials listed in the preceding article. The term "elected person" shall refer to a candidate who has obtained the legally required number of votes and has been elected as any of the autonomous officials listed in the preceding article. (Article 4) The term "assembly" as used in this Law shall refer to the township assembly and town assembly prescribed in the Township and Town Autonomy Implementation Law, and the neighborhood assembly prescribed in the City Organization Law. (Article 5) The term "citizen" as used in this Law shall refer to the township citizen and town citizen prescribed in the Township and Town Autonomy Implementation Law, and the city citizen prescribed in the City Organization Law.

Chapter II: Elections. (Article 6) The date of the election of autonomous officials shall be determined in the agenda of the assembly, except in the case of a re-election due to a recall. The aforementioned agenda shall be announced or delivered to each citizen seven days before the opening of the assembly. (Article 7) The district office shall appoint one election supervisor, and a certain number of ballot administrators and ballot counters within five days before the election, and report it for record. Citizens of this township, this town, or this neighborhood shall not be the aforementioned supervisor or administrator. (Article 8) The election supervisor shall guide and supervise the administrator in handling the voting and counting of ballots. (Article 9) The duties of the ballot administrator are as follows: 1. To be in charge of the ballot box, ballots, and voter roster. 2. To maintain order during voting. (Article 10) The duties of the ballot counter are as follows: 1. To calculate the number of votes. 2. To check the authenticity of the ballots. 3. To determine whether a ballot is legal. 4. To maintain order during the counting of ballots. 5. To preserve the ballots. (Article 11) Within fifteen days before the delivery of the assembly agenda, the township office, town office, or neighborhood office shall announce the names of citizens at the entrance of the office. Within five days after the announcement, if there are any omissions or errors, the person concerned or a related person may request a correction. The aforementioned request for correction shall be made with supporting documents. Two copies of the corrected citizen roster shall be made, one submitted to the district office and one submitted by the district office to the county government or municipal government for record. (Article 12) After the announcement period in the preceding article expires, the township office, town office, or neighborhood office shall prepare a voter roster according to the citizen roster, and record the name, gender, age, and residence of each citizen. (Article 13) Those whose age or residence period reaches the requirements for citizenship at the time of the opening of the assembly may register by taking the citizen oath before the announcement of the citizen's name. (Article 14) Fifteen days before the opening of the assembly, those who have the qualifications to be a candidate, and whose election has been suspended in accordance with the provisions of Article 11, Paragraph 2 of the Township and Town Autonomy Implementation Law or Article 48 of the City Organization Law, may, if the reason for the suspension no longer exists, request the removal of the restriction on suspension of election by obtaining supporting documents. After accepting the aforementioned request, the township office, town office, or neighborhood office shall, in addition to making a public announcement, report it to the district office, which shall forward it to the county government or municipal government for approval. (Article 15) The election of autonomous officials shall be held in installments in accordance with the following provisions: 1. The township assembly shall first elect the township chief, then the township supervisory committee members. 2. The town assembly shall first elect the town chief, then the town supervisory committee members. 3. The neighborhood assembly shall first elect the neighborhood head, then the neighborhood supervisory committee members. In the first and second provisions of the preceding paragraph, the one with the second-highest number of votes in the election of the township chief and town chief shall be the deputy township chief or deputy town chief. (Article 16) The ballot paper and ballot box shall be made by the district office according to the prescribed form, and handed over to the township office, town office, or neighborhood office seven days before the opening of the assembly. The ballot paper shall list the names of all candidates, and the order of names shall be determined by lottery. (Unfinished)

Three Routes for the Fujian Army to Suppress the Lu Troops 54

The Provincial Government Establishes a Temporary Military Affairs Office

And Establishes a Fuzhou Martial Law Command

Fuzhou Dispatch: After Chairman Yang returned to Fujian, he has met with Commander-in-Chief Chen and Marshal Liu several times regarding the military suppression of Lu's troops. As a result, the provincial government has increased the establishment of a temporary military affairs office, with Yang Tingying, Chief of Staff of the Army Headquarters, as the director, and Li Guangzhao, Senior Staff Officer of the 56th Division, as the deputy director. Yin Jiaxun, Yang Guangxun, and Zheng Yulin are appointed as advisors. The office is divided into two sections: security and confidential affairs. The security section remains as originally established by the provincial government, while the confidential affairs section is headed by Wang Fu as the section chief, with Shi Leng and others as staff members. In addition, a martial law command is established, jointly headed by Liu Shangzhi and Li Dingzhang, the Brigade Commander and Deputy Brigade Commander of the 167th Brigade of Liu's Division, respectively. Both have already assumed their positions yesterday. The martial law command has also issued martial law regulations. The joint temporary military police office has been abolished. As for the three-pronged deployment for attacking Lu, it is briefly described as follows:

Liu's Division's Side: Liu's Division, seeing that Lu's troops are gradually retreating, is preparing to advance. At noon on the 12th, a mortar company and a machine gun company moved from the city to the North Gate and, after spending the night there, proceeded to Xiaobeiling. On the 13th, the 2nd Battalion of the 333rd Regiment of the 167th Brigade followed. The 335th Regiment of the 168th Brigade is deployed from Xiaoling to the vicinity of Hongshan Bridge. The 3rd Battalion of the 333rd Regiment of the 167th Brigade moved from Hongshan Bridge to Xiaobeiling for deployment. The troops on the western route are also advancing upstream from Tongkou Ganche. The 331st Regiment in the rear has completed the renovation of the wartime relics in the Xiaobeiling, Maotou Mountain, and Dafu Ridge areas. In addition to leaving a part of the troops stationed in various high mountains of Xiaobei, they have also been dispatched to the front line. Deputy Division Commander Yan Er'ai is in Nanjing negotiating with the central military authorities to send the newly formed Zhan Brigade to assist in the battle. They are expected to arrive in Fujian soon. It is also said that the Central Zhao Brigade stationed in Zhejiang has been ordered to come to Fujian and is also preparing to depart.

Naval Side: The right wing of the attack on Lu is undertaken by the Marine Corps. Currently, although Lu's troops in the Nan'gang area have retreated from the Shatidi and Milaoshan areas, the Zhu Regiment of Lu Xinming's troops and the Su Qinzi and Wu Da'ang and Li Jinshui factions of Sun Guozhen's troops are still responsible for supplying food locally. Chairman Yang yesterday specifically ordered Lin Shouguo, the Brigade Commander of the 2nd Marine Brigade, to lead Lin Bingzhou's unit of the 3rd Regiment, supplemented by two mountain gun and machine gun battalions, to land at Nan'gang and advance from the side. Commander-in-Chief Chen also personally inspected the Haihu and other gunboats on the morning before yesterday and personally instructed Chen Wenlin, the captain of the air squadron, on the tactics of aerial combat, dispatching seaplanes to cover the Marine Corps' departure from the due south. However, 250 porters are needed, with a porterage fee of 20 yuan per person, and the Municipal Public Security Bureau is instructed to relay this to the police stations No. 1 and No. 5 to recruit them for standby. Lin himself intends to go to the front to command the troops immediately. In addition, the troops of the 2nd Marine Brigade stationed in the province, in Zhongzhou, Guanyin Well, Cangqian Mountain, Xiadu, and north of the bridge in Nantai, as well as in the Taijiang Xun and Bai Ma Wang Temple and Minqing Hall areas of Yazhou, are responsible for the rear defense line. They have now also been ordered to move to Shangbeiling for concentration. The special service company, machine gun company, and mountain gun team originally stationed in the Shijinci and Nan'gang districts are also approved to open provinces for collection, and the defense area left behind Chen Commander-in-Chief Chen has ordered Jin Zhenzhong of the First Brigade to dispatch the Jin Zhensheng Battalion from Funing to the province to take over the Taijiang area first, and it is said that Lin Shouguo intends to ask the First Brigade to draw a battalion from each regiment to go to the front enemy. Lin is to go to Xiamen today to consult with Lin Guogeng, Fang Shengtao, and others on military matters.

Southern Fujian Side: Since Fang Shengtao's return to Fujian this time, it has long been rumored that he will be ordered to command a regiment of Zhang Zhen's division and Xiao Shuxuan's regiment of Chen Guohui's brigade to jointly attack Lu's troops. The provincial government yesterday appointed Fang as a special military commissioner, and both the national and provincial troops in southern Fujian are under his control and dispatch. It is now heard that a part of Zhang Zhen's troops and Xiao's regiment will begin to move out. Chen Guohui will also be stationed in Anxi Xianwan, Penglai, and Yingnei. Approximately 1,000 of his own troops have been transferred to Yongchun for concentration, preparing to be the vanguard in the future attack on Lu. However, at the same time, the issue of Chen Guohui and Gao Jingli competing for the Quanzhou territory and the issue of Chen's troops replenishing supplies and ammunition are still under negotiation.

Summarizing the above situation, the front of Liu's Division and the side of Lin's Brigade will most likely move out first, advancing through the Min and Gu counties. Central troops can also arrive continuously. To quickly resolve the military affairs against Lu's troops, Chairman Yang has changed the airport to the Wangzhuang Agricultural Experiment Field and has printed 10,000 small leaflets urging Lu's troops to return, which were dropped this morning from the Haihu and Haihu aircraft to the positions of Lu's troops upstream. Those who bring a platoon to return will still be appointed as platoon leaders, and those who bring a company to return will still be appointed as company commanders, and so on up to a battalion or regiment, all will be accepted and never implicated. Otherwise, both good and bad will be destroyed, and there will be no chance to regret it, etc. (16th)

Dispute over the Head of Fujian Finance Department 55

He Gonggan Defends Himself as Not Being a Nationalist

Fuzhou Dispatch: After Yang Shuzhuang returned to Fujian, in order to reorganize finance, he specifically recommended He Gonggan, the former Secretary-General of the Provincial Government and Salt Transport Envoy, to act as the Director of the Finance Department and Special Financial Commissioner, ordering him to be responsible for maintaining it. The Ministry of Finance approved the telegram and ordered him to take over the position and report it. However, on the day the Ministry's telegram arrived in the province, Gan Yun and Feng Ji'an, two guiding committee members of the Provincial Party Department, strongly opposed He's appointment in the General Memorial Week report and in the articles of the "Republic Daily News," because He had previously handled the "Orphan Army Magazine," which contained nationalist colors. At the same time, a leaflet titled "30 Million People of Fujian" was found in the city, strongly attacking He and favoring Tang Dunbo, the current acting secretary in charge of the Finance Department (Tang has resigned several times due to his inability to maintain the position). This has attracted social attention. Yang Shuzhuang originally intended to follow the telegram from the Finance Ministry and order He to take office on the 18th to ensure that someone would take charge as soon as possible. Upon hearing the news, Gan and Feng notified Chen Shoufan, the Secretary of the Provincial Government, by telephone on the afternoon of the 17th, asking him to persuade Yang Shuzhuang to dissuade him. Yang immediately dispatched Chen Peikun, a member of the Provincial Committee, to the Provincial Party Department to consult with Feng and Gan. As a result, He was ordered to postpone taking office, and the Provincial Party Department and the Provincial Government telegraphed the Central National Government to request instructions and wait for a reply before deciding on a solution. However, He Gonggan remained extremely calm. Yesterday, a reporter from a certain newspaper visited He at his private residence and asked for his opinion on the current situation. He replied that whether he is a nationalist is proven by the facts and does not need to be argued. As for the "Orphan Army Magazine," it was initiated by Chen Chengze, bringing together scholars from various factions to publish their political views in writing. Therefore, Zhou Fo Hai, Luo Jialun, Shi Weihuan, Zeng Qi, Guo Moruo, and others have contributed. Later, due to differences in opinion, it disintegrated, and the magazine was also discontinued. There have been more than just this one attack on me for being a nationalist. When I served as the Director of the Propaganda Department in 1927, some people also pointed out that I and Liu Wendao, the Deputy Director of the Political Department at the time, were both Nationalists.

Fierce Battle Between Quanzhou Militia and Gao's Troops 56

Xiamen Dispatch: Since Lu Xingbang's rebellion and the transfer of the 56th Division's Chen Wantai Brigade stationed in Quanzhou to the province, Quanzhou has been taken over by Gao Weiguo's guerrilla brigade. Gao is a compilation of bandits from Nan'an and Hui'an counties. Recently, he has been collecting funds from Jinjiang and Nan'an counties, leading to a joint resistance by the militia of the two counties. They attacked Quanzhou city on the night of the 10th and withdrew on the 11th. For several days, Gao's troops and the militia have been facing off. The number of militiamen continuing to gather has reached over 1,000. They attacked the city again on the 17th, but were defeated and retreated.

Earlier, Gao collected funds from various villages. He collected 20,000 yuan each from the three villages of Qingmang, Xialian, and Chendian outside the Xinmen Gate of Quanzhou City. The village of Shudou, which has many overseas Chinese, is the richest, and he collected 50 catties of 10-yuan banknotes from the Bank of China (approximately 80,000 to 90,000 yuan) and detained more than 40 residents of the village, limiting the four villages to hand over the funds within three days. The militia of each village was greatly angered and unanimously decided to resist. One day before the deadline, the militia of Qingmang, Xialian, Chendian, and Shudou in the southern district of the outer city, approximately 600 people, gathered together. In the afternoon of the 10th, more than 100 people, dressed in plain clothes and carrying short guns, disguised themselves as gamblers and vendors and infiltrated Quanzhou city through the Xinxi and Liangmen gates. At the appointed time, they coordinated from within. At about 11 o'clock that night, another 400 people in plain clothes, each carrying a rifle, advanced in three routes towards the Xinmen, Ximen, and Nanmen gates. Shudou is only 10 li away from the city and arrived before midnight. More than 100 people from each of the three routes first attacked the gates. Gao's troops guarding the city had only one platoon at Ximen, and all were disarmed. A company at Xinmen was caught off guard and disarmed more than 20 and killed or wounded more than 10. A company stationed at the Xinqiaowei station at Nanmen was also killed two soldiers, wounded seven or eight people, and seized more than 10 guns. All three routes were unprepared, and Gao's troops suffered heavy losses. The militia then advanced towards the city. At about 12 o'clock at midnight, the plainclothes team inside the city responded and cut through the gates, entering the city in three routes. The city was in an uproar. Gao Weiguo and his subordinates stationed in various places did not know the enemy's strength and, moreover, it was late at night, so they dared not fight and hurriedly withdrew from the North Gate. The militia entered the city and searched everywhere. When they arrived at Gao's headquarters in the Xin Ya at about 1:30 in the morning, it was about 3:00 in the morning, and the sky was about to dawn. The militia retreated out of the city, gathering at Xinqiao and Fuqiao, and retreating towards Shudou. The sky was not yet bright when they left, because the Shudou and Xin District militia were impulsive this time and had no contact with other villages in advance. They feared that Gao's troops would counterattack at dawn and it would be difficult to defend without reinforcements. In this battle, Gao's troops were killed 50 or 60 people and more than 90 rifles and two machine guns were seized. Gao Weiguo retreated to Wu Bu Camp and Xiajing outside the North Gate to gather his troops. He learned that the attackers were militia and not many in number. At about 5:00 at dawn, he returned to the city through the North Gate and conducted a major search for the insiders. Three militia soldiers who had fallen behind were captured, all of whom were northerners, and beheaded. Also, because the Mauser company of his troops were all northerners and had defected to the militia, he searched for northerners in the city, and more than 30 were killed. Desheng and Mingde money shops opened by Shudou villagers on South Street were robbed of more than 20,000 yuan, and more than 10 shopkeepers were arrested and sent to Gao's hometown of Fushanyao. Chen Zhengjia, a doctor at Wenling Hospital, was beheaded because he had a private telephone with Shudou Village for medical treatment, and Gao suspected that he had notified Shudou that the city was unprepared, leading them to attack the city. On the 11th, 12th, and 13th, Quanzhou City was a world of terror, with people being killed, houses burned, and looted. Those who fled to Xiamen were continuous. Quanzhou City was completely closed on the 11th and 12th. On the 13th, Gao ordered the shops to open, but no one dared to respond. The Quanzhou-Anhai bus service was completely interrupted on the 11th and 12th and only resumed on the 13th. After this incident occurred, the militia of Jinjiang and Nan'an counties formed a major alliance. On the 12th, they telegraphed the province, "Sent to the Provincial Party Department, the Provincial Government, Chairman Yang, Division Commander Liu, He Ding, Commander Chen, and Ji Liang for review: Since Gao Weiguo was stationed in Quanzhou, he has been collecting funds and loans harshly, and abducting people up to 40 at a time, disturbing the people to the extreme. Recently, he has even intensified his efforts, coercing Shudou Village, which has many merchants doing business in Surabaya and is known to be wealthy, to hand over 50 catties of banknotes. Yesterday, the villagers, unable to bear the pressure, resisted and sought survival in death. Now everyone is in danger. Please quickly send formal troops to Quanzhou to be stationed and appease the people. If you cannot immediately find a way to relieve the people, we will unite and save ourselves by fighting the bandits. We also ask for the supply of bullets and practical support. The telegram is extremely urgent." The joint militia of the Nan District, Xin District, Shudou District, Qingyang District, Shishi District, Yamenkou District, Yongning District, Tanying District, Guanqiao District, Shuitou District, and Lianshi District of Jinjiang County, at the same time, the Jinjiang County Party Department also telegraphed the province, "Sent to the Provincial Party Department, the Provincial Government, Chairman Yang, Division Commander Liu, and Commander Chen for review: The bandit Gao is stationed in Quanzhou, looting, extorting, abusing, and killing without a day of rest, and the people are displaced. Recently, he has intensified his efforts and coerced Shudou Village to hand over 50 catties of banknotes. In one day, he abducted dozens of residents of the outer city. His cruelty has aroused the resistance of the people. The day Gao's troops and the people fought fiercely, and the killings were tragic. Today, he also abducted and killed more than 30 innocent northerners in the city. Now the order in Quanzhou City is in chaos, and the lives of the people cannot be protected. Please quickly send elite troops to severely punish and suppress them to relieve the suffering." The Jinjiang County Party Department.

On the 13th, Gao sent troops to station in Qingyang again and sent a team to attack Shudou, but on the same day, the militia from Shishi, Yongning, and Yamenkou in the Jinjiang Nanmen area also gathered in Shishi, divided into five teams, including a rifle team and a plainclothes pistol team, approximately 400 people, advanced to Qingyang on the 14th. Gao hurriedly withdrew the troops from Anhai and Qingyang back to Quanzhou, and the team attacking Shudou also withdrew halfway. By the 16th, the militia in Qingyang had advanced to Dongshan Village, only two or three li away from the Nanmen of Quanzhou. At present, the militia outside Nanmen has gathered six teams, approximately 600 people, from Dongshan Village to Anhai and Yongning, all under their control. The militia and Shudou and other villages outside Xinmen have also gathered 600 people, and these two sides each have a reserve team of 400 or 500 people. The meeting on the 16th decided to attack the city again. In the early morning of the 17th, the militia on the Nanmen side was in charge of two routes. One route, led by the commander Huang Jinyan, attacked the Nanmen with more than 300 people. The deputy commander Xu Wenqi led more than 200 people to attack Tumen. The militia of 400 people from Shudou and other villages outside Xinmen, led by Jiang Guangtie and Xie Guanghui, attacked the Xinmen and Ximen. At about 3:00 in the morning before dawn, the three routes launched a fierce attack, and the fighting continued until about 7:00 in the morning. The militia led by Huang Jinyan had rushed to the Xinqiao at the Nanmen entrance. Gao's troops retreated into the city, and Huang feared that Gao had an ambush, so he dared not enter immediately. At about 9:00, Gao transferred a large team of reinforcements from Honglai to counterattack out of the city. The fighting continued until 10:00, Huang was no match and retreated to Dongshan Village. Xu Wenqi, who attacked Tumen, had broken into the city to the Tianhou Palace. Because the Nanmen retreated, he also withdrew immediately. At the Xinmen and Ximen, Gao first burned and cut off trees, and also withdrew at the same time. At present, the militia is preparing for a third attack. (July 18th)

Conflict Between Bandit Troops and Red Spear Society in Jiaoxian 57

Qingdao Dispatch: The bandit troops entrenched in Jiaoxian know that they are not tolerated by the people. They have repeatedly sent people to Han Fuju to request that they be reorganized and incorporated into the Second Mixed Brigade of the First Army Corps, and that the bandit leader Ji Xiaoxi be appointed as the brigade commander. Ji has already issued a telegram on the 16th to take office. Unexpectedly, after being reorganized by the Han army, these bandits thought they had become formal troops, extorting and looting even more than before. On the 16th, the bandit leader Sun Hanchen, currently serving as the commander of the bandit army group, led dozens of bandits to the southern villages of Jiaoxian, extorting money from each village under the pretext of collecting tobacco taxes. When they reached the vicinity of Shiwulikuang, they happened to meet the local Red Spear Society, and a conflict broke out between the two sides. After several hours of fierce fighting, seven people were killed and several injured on the Red Spear Society side. The bandit leader Sun Hanchen was also stabbed several times and was rescued back to the city by the bandits. Not long after, he died of his injuries. The bandits were greatly angered and emptied the city on the 17th to avenge Sun. They surrounded the villages near Shiwulikuang, intending to gather and kill. The bandits were powerful. After only a few hours of fighting, the Red Spear Society was defeated and retreated to the rear. Women and children who were unable to escape in time were tragically killed. The bandits returned to the city in victory and dismembered the four captured members of the Red Spear Society to offer as sacrifices to Sun Bandit's spirit. After the Red Spear Society's tragic defeat, they were saddened by the destruction of their homes and the slaughter of their wives and children, so they sought help from all the villages. The militia of each village was also deeply afraid of being affected by the cruelty of the bandit army. For the sake of self-defense, they will unite the militia of the entire county, attack the county seat, and fight the bandits to the death. They are currently in the process of carrying out this plan. The bandit side is also on high alert. They have tightly closed the four gates and driven all the merchants and residents of the city to the city walls to defend, while the bandits take turns resting. According to refugees who escaped from Jiaoxian City, the bandit army is currently extorting 20,000 yuan from the gentry and merchants in the city to prepare for Sun Bandit's memorial service. Sun Bandit has been embalmed, and the coffin used is the burial object of the mother of Wang, the richest man in Jiaoyi, worth more than a thousand yuan. The bandits have driven the merchants and residents to defend the city, leaving only women in their homes. The bandits enter and leave the people's homes at will, and forcibly rape those who are slightly attractive. Jiaoxian City is now in a deep and hot place. I hope the officials will save them. (July 18th)

Investigation of the Black Mountain Snake Fossil 58

After the discovery of snake fossils in Black Mountain, Hanyang, the Academia Sinica, upon receiving a letter from the Hanyang Municipal Engineering Bureau requesting the dispatch of personnel for research, immediately sent Shu Wenbo, an assistant researcher at the Institute of Geology of the Academia Sinica, to Hanyang the day before yesterday. At 10:00 yesterday morning, Chen Pengguan, a technician from the Engineering Bureau, along with Xiang Dao and others, accompanied Shu by car to Black Mountain to conduct an on-site investigation. A reporter from the Riri News Company, believing that this matter was of great value in scientific research,

also went to observe with them. The situation is recorded as follows:

General Situation of Black Mountain: Black Mountain, formerly known as He Mountain, is located about three li northwest of Hanyang, with the Yangtze River behind it to the north. It stands opposite Turtle and Snake Mountains. It is about one li in circumference and about seven or eight zhang in height. According to legend, this mountain once collapsed during the Tang Dynasty, so the quarrying of stones has been prohibited throughout history, but this cannot be verified.

A Glimpse of the Fossil: From the foot of the mountain to the mountainside, stones with fish scale patterns can be found, winding to the top of the mountain. However, most of them have been destroyed by the stone workers, leaving only their discontinuous remnants. The excavated fossil is three sides, and the fish scale pattern is extremely clear. Shu's Remarks: Black Mountain in Hanyang is a slightly metamorphic sandstone layer, similar to Snake Mountain in Wuchang, and belongs to the "Jurassic Period." When the city of Hanyang was quarrying stones in Black Mountain, fossils were found with a diameter of two to three inches and obvious scales. Everyone thought they were insects, but since the rock layer of the mountain is Jurassic and leaf fossils have also been found, shaped like fans or light, the so-called insect is not accurate. It seems to be the remains of a tree trunk. It is planned to move this stone to a detailed research institute, and the age of the rock layer of the mountain can be determined. I still need to go to Black Mountain again within a few days to conduct a second investigation. (Riri News Agency)

Sharp Decline in Revenue of South Manchuria Railway After Joint Transportation of Four Routes in Northeast 59

Exceeded 4 Million Yuan

Shenyang Dispatch: After the implementation of joint transportation by the four state-owned railways in Northeast China, the price of gold soared. The passenger and freight fares of Chinese railways are still calculated in silver dollars, which is more than half the price of South Manchuria Railway trains. Therefore, all passenger and freight transportation that is not absolutely necessary has been switched to state-owned railways. In addition, recently, the Beining Railway has been newly painted, decorated, and renovated for all levels of vehicles. Its cleanliness and safety are no less than that of South Manchuria Railway trains. With cheap prices and high quality, not only Chinese people are happy to take them, but foreigners also praise them. Therefore, the business of each road has suddenly become active, and it is quite overwhelmed. As a result, the South Manchuria Railway is showing a state of decline, and its revenue has sharply declined. Although the South Manchuria Railway authorities are trying to find ways to remedy this, it is impossible to save it in fact due to the continued increase in the price of gold. According to the temporary statistics released by the South Manchuria Railway Survey Division, the business income as of the 7th of this month has decreased compared with the income in the same period last year. The amount of the decrease is listed as follows:

Income as of the 6th of this month - Income in the same period last year - Comparison Increase or Decrease

22.94 - 26.96 - 4.023.

6.845 - 9.958 - 113 yuan

yuan yuan

Income as of the 7th of this month - Income in the same period last year - Comparison Increase or Decrease

23.11 - 27.19 - 4.077.

8.370 - 6.293 - 923 yuan

yuan yuan

Looking at the above table, the business of the South Manchuria Railway is indeed showing a very large decrease and is getting worse. It is clear at a glance that the amount of the decrease has already exceeded 4 million yuan. If the state-owned railways in Northeast China can take the opportunity to continue to improve and seek to regain their rights and interests, they can achieve twice the result with half the effort. The future decrease in revenue of the South Manchuria Railway is unknown, which is enough to attract general attention. Jiangsu Province Penalizes Late Payment of Rush Tribute 60

Restoration of Cases Before 1916

In Jiangsu Province, fines for late payment of rush tribute have been collected. Since the first year of the Republic, the original deadline was two months for completion of payment. Overdue payments were subject to an additional 10% penalty. In 1916, the Provincial Assembly resolved to change it to an additional 20% after the two-month deadline, followed by another two-month extension, after which an additional 10% would be charged. This has been implemented since the upper rush in 1917 and has not changed until now. The Department of Finance now believes that the levy of rush tribute in Jiangsu Province is late, and the regulation of a two-month deadline is appropriate. However, the issue of late payment fines has caused obstacles to the levy. Moreover, the levy of lower rush tribute cannot be started early due to the autumn survey. After the initial and subsequent deadlines, the year has ended. Therefore, less than half of the collection is completed at the time of cutoff, which is bound to be included in old debts and may even be lost after a long time. After careful consideration, it is necessary to restore the old cases before 1916. It is specially requested that the provincial government, starting from the 19th year, impose an additional penalty of 10% after two months from the start of the levy and order a simple procedure for late payment fines to warn against fatigue. This has been approved by the Provincial Committee. The summary is recorded as follows: (1) The counties should collect rush tribute and reed taxes in accordance with the cases before 1916, and the deadline shall be two months from the date of commencement of the levy. Overdue payments shall be subject to an additional 10% late payment fine. (2) Starting from the upper rush levy in the 19th year, after deducting two months, the penalty shall be implemented, and no extension shall be allowed for any reason. (3) The additional penalty shall be limited to the regular provincial and county taxes, and various additional taxes collected shall not be penalized. (4) Two months after the start of the levy, each county shall clearly demarcate the various items of rush tribute and reed tax that have been collected, cut off the numbers, and report them for inspection. (5) This fine shall be fully used for provincial use in accordance with the cases before 1916, and the counties shall not retain it. (6) The old system of charging an additional 20% for the initial two-month deadline and an additional 10% for the subsequent two-month deadline shall be abolished immediately. (7) One month after the penalty period, if the payment is not made, the payment shall be ordered to be recovered.

Wuhu Express News 61

Wuhu City Police Chief Yu Mingxun has been ordered to transfer to the province. The vacancy will be filled by Tang Shaogao. Tang is currently the Chief of the General Affairs Section of the Provincial Government and will arrive in Wuhu to take office in the coming days. However, various sectors in Wuhu are concerned that during Yu's tenure, he levied an additional 20% surcharge on shop and residential property rentals. He purchased 51 automatic box-type pistols, 25,000 rounds of ammunition, 25 Browning pistols, 5,000 rounds of ammunition, 4 German rifles, 3 Hubei-made rifles, and 18 bicycles. These were originally purchased with local public funds for local public security. To prevent future loss, a meeting was held yesterday at the Public Security Bureau to discuss storage methods. It was decided that the city and county Party headquarters, the municipal preparatory office, the county government, the general chamber of commerce, and the county education bureau would jointly manage the equipment. The Public Security Bureau will issue a receipt for the borrowed items, and the words "Wuhu City" will be branded on them. A report will also be submitted to the provincial government for record-keeping. No one will be allowed to remove the items in the future.

The Provincial Federation of Commerce and the Wuhu Sundries Guild are opposing the sugar tax and the newly appointed Director-General of the Sugar Tax Bureau, Gao Peide. Due to the unfavorable situation, Gao has returned to Beijing from Wuhu. Currently, the Sundries Guild reports that the sugar tax has recently been intensified, with an import tax of 1.3 taels and an export tax of 0.67 taels. The sugar tax has also been increased to over one yuan. The guild has petitioned the Anhui Financial Commissioner's Office to abolish it completely. In addition to petitioning the central government, the Provincial Federation of Commerce has sent telegrams to 60 county chambers of commerce throughout the province, urging them to work together to fight against the tax.

The Wuhu County Government has been ordered to establish a public property clearing committee. It has been decided that one representative from the county Party headquarters, the county government, the financial management office, the education bureau, the defense corps, and each autonomous region will form the committee. The committee is expected to complete the clearing within one month and hand it over to the financial management office for management. However, educational properties are not included in this process.

Recent weather in southern Anhui has been favorable for agriculture, and a good harvest is expected. Stored rice in the countryside is being transported to the city for sale. Rice prices have fallen from about seventeen yuan to about fourteen yuan in the past two weeks. The price stabilization committee is now planning to conclude the operations of the various price stabilization bureaus.

The Anhui Financial Commissioner's Office will hold a meeting of all likin bureau chiefs on the 21st to reorganize the likin tax collection. The bureau chiefs are arriving in Wuhu. Financial Commissioner Lou Fu returned to Wuhu from Beijing yesterday to attend the meeting. (19th)

Songjiang 62

Ke Guanyin, the Executive Committee Member of the County Education Association and Mayor of Guyang Town, has been dismissed due to mental illness. Jiading 63

An adulterous woman poisons her husband. Shen Ajin, a farmer in Xinqiao Village, Anding Township, Jiading, married a woman surnamed Zhou from a neighboring village. After marriage, they lived peacefully. Last year, Zhou had an affair with Zhang Aquan from the village and saw her husband as an eyesore. On the 19th, she mixed mercury into fried noodles and fed it to Ajin. Ajin did not notice at first. After eating half of it, he felt the taste was bad and could not swallow it. He fed it to his dog. Seeing the large amount of mercury in the noodles, he knew what his wife had done. He was furious, slapped her several times, and turned her over to the defense corps, requesting strict punishment. After a preliminary hearing by the district chief, Zhou confessed that she was instigated by Zhang Aquan. Zhang Aquan was also arrested and brought to the corps, but he denied the affair. On the 20th, both men and women were sent to the county for trial.

Suzhou 64

Detailed Report on the Incident Involving Wounded Soldiers and the Subsequent Martial Law and the Cracking Down on Communists. The situation, which involved wounded soldiers causing trouble, the declaration of martial law, and the arrest of communists, was resolved yesterday (21st). A detailed report follows: On the evening of the 18th, at 8 PM, the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau received a tip that foreign communists Zhu Jicheng and Wang Guangming were active on Changmen Road. Patrol Officer Zhang Shousong was dispatched to investigate the Zhonghua Hotel. He found Zhu Jicheng in Room 81 on the third floor. Zhang immediately opened a room near Room 81 and instructed the tea boy to inform him if anyone called for Zhu. After a while, a call came. Zhang answered, but the other party did not recognize his voice as Zhu's and refused to say what it was about, then hung up. After investigation, the call was found to have come from Room 27 of the Xinxin Hotel. Knowing the whereabouts of the group, Zhang rushed back to the bureau and dispatched Flying Squad Patrol Chief Liu Zhanmin to lead a team to arrest Zhu. He also reported to the joint military-police-group investigation office, which sent a team to search the Xinxin Hotel. Wang Guangming, Xu Yuanzhang, and eleven wounded soldiers were arrested in Rooms 19, 20, and 29. Eighty-eight small flags and symbols were found in the rooms. After being taken to the investigation office, they confessed that they planned to seize weapons from the military and police, then set fire to the prison and occupy Suzhou City, with the riot scheduled for 10 AM on the 19th. They were detained for further investigation. The director of the bureau reported to the county government, which forwarded the report to both Beijing and Shanghai for instructions. On the evening of the 19th, the commander of the Third Regiment of the Guard Brigade, Shi Juemin, received a call from the capital's brigade headquarters, stating that Beijing had learned of the communists' planned riot in Suzhou on that day and instructed him to be prepared and to close the city gates early at 9 AM. Commander Shi was preparing to comply when a disturbance occurred outside the city. Previously, at around 5 PM, Battalion Commander Lou Yue of the Second Battalion of the Guard Brigade was returning from outside the city in a car when he saw dozens of wounded soldiers armed with iron bars and knives lurking in Ciyi Lane behind the General Post Office. Seeing Lou pass by alone, they verbally abused him and surrounded him. Lou, realizing the danger, got out of the car and used one hand to push the car forward for cover while using the other to threaten them with a pistol. The crowd did not retreat and continued to attack with weapons. Lou fired a shot, hitting one person in the leg. The others became even more violent, knowing that Battalion Commander Lou did not have many bullets. One wounded soldier struck Lou on the head with a heavy iron bar. Lou quickly fired another shot, hitting the attacker in the right side, and the bar fell to the ground. Lou then took the opportunity to escape to the Daxin Hotel. More than a hundred wounded soldiers surrounded the Daxin Hotel. Fortunately, the investigation office arrived and the crowd dispersed. On the 20th, all the guards outside Changmen Gate went on strike. On the morning of the 21st, the 17th Rear Hospital was surrounded. The instructor and the transportation battalion were responsible for sealing off the area and setting up machine guns at key points near the hospital. The Public Security Bureau's Flying Squad, the 4th Police Company of the County, and the Merchant Corps were responsible for patrol and security. Guard Battalion Commander Zhou Wenbin led a team to the hospital to distribute discharge pay of five yuan to each of the 400 lightly wounded and recovered wounded soldiers. They were divided into groups and taken to the station, where they boarded 15 vehicles and left for Nanjing at 1 PM. (About 40 people escaped along the way to Wangting when the vehicles stopped). There are still hundreds of wounded in the 17th Hospital, but they are all seriously wounded, so the area is no longer dangerous. It is reported that the decision to discharge the troublemaking wounded soldiers from Suzhou was made by officials from various agencies at the joint investigation office the day before (20th).

Among them, Wang Qingfa suffered the greatest loss. Zhang Housheng, Li Zifang, Shao Shouquan, and Chen Ronggui were injured by the bandits. Afterwards, the people of the town went to the county to complain and requested that the bandits be arrested.

Education Budget for Jiangsu Province in the 19th Year (3) 76

(4) Distribution Method of Special Project Funds for Primary and Secondary Schools in the 19th Year

(1) Military Training Equipment Subsidy of 15,000 yuan, 100 yuan per high school grade (limited to equipment for public use), totaling the amount on the right.

(2) Boy Scout Equipment Subsidy of 9,000 yuan, 60 yuan per junior high school grade (limited to equipment for public use), totaling the amount on the right.

(3) Rural Normal School Promotion Project Subsidy of 3,000 yuan, 500 yuan per school, totaling the amount on the right for the whole year.

(4) Agricultural and Sericultural School Promotion Project and Practice Subsidy of 6,000 yuan, 2,000 yuan per school, totaling the amount on the right for the whole year.

(5) Local Education Guidance Funds for Provincial Experimental Primary Schools of 22,500 yuan. Each provincial experimental primary school will establish one local education guidance officer, with salary, travel expenses, printing expenses, etc., totaling 1,500 yuan per school per year (the regulations will be determined separately), totaling the amount on the right.

(6) Field Trip Subsidy of 6,000 yuan, limited to third-year students of the general and business departments of high schools, with a subsidy of 5 silver yuan per person. The province will have 30 grades, with 40 people per grade, totaling the amount on the right.

(7) Normal School Student Visit Subsidy of 8,000 yuan, limited to graduating students of the high school normal department and rural normal department, with a subsidy of 8 yuan per person. The province will have 25 grades, with 40 people per grade, totaling the amount on the right.

(8) Travel Expenses for Participating in Provincial Games of 5,000 yuan, limited to those who attend the games, with a standard of 10 yuan per person (the actual disbursement will still depend on the distance of the road to determine the standard of subsidy). There will be 500 participants in the province, totaling the amount on the right.

(9) Travel Miscellaneous Expenses for Participating in Boy Scout Review of 2,500 yuan. The boat and car expenses for the Boy Scouts going to Beijing for review will be exempted as in the 18th year. The remaining travel miscellaneous expenses will be subsidized at 5 yuan per person. The number of participants in the province will be 500, totaling the amount on the right.

(10) Travel Expenses for Participating in Various Public Meetings Called by the Department (such as Achievement Exhibitions, Various Competitions, etc.) of 5,000 yuan, calculated based on half the number of participants in the sports meeting, with two times a year, totaling the amount on the right.

(11) Education Expenses for Children of Revolutionary Martyrs of 3,000 yuan. In addition to the exemption of tuition and accommodation fees, which are not listed as income, all meals and miscellaneous fees that should be exempted will be 100 yuan per person. There will be 30 people in the province, totaling the amount on the right. (12) Other Temporary Project Expenses of 15,000 yuan. For temporary projects added to various schools by the Department's order, the expenses of which are not listed in the budget, the above expenses will be used to offset them. The distribution method will be determined and announced by the Department at any time.

For items (1) to (5) above, each school will follow the above standards and list a separate item for special project expenses in the regular expense budget, and submit a plan for use after approval. The funds will be allocated monthly at the same time as the regular expenses. For items (6) to (11), each school will follow the above standards and submit a plan for approval when needed. (End)

The Ending of the School Unrest at Suzhou Women's Middle School and Experimental Primary School 77

President Tian of Suzhou Women's Middle School and Experimental Primary School resigned because of the complicated situation and bad elements in the school, as reported in this newspaper. It is reported that the resignation has been approved by the Department and will be completed immediately. He has agreed with the new president, Chen Dingxiu, to hand over the school on the 26th of this month. It is learned that President Chen has recently been instructed by the Department to thoroughly rectify and reform the school. Therefore, he will no longer reappoint the male teachers who led the trouble, including Jiang Weikun (also known as Bohou), Jin Fen (also known as Zufeng), Chen Liuzong, Guo Changluo, Jiang Pinzhen, Ding Jiongpei, and Pan Youlin, and the female teachers Zhang Yutong (also known as Baiping), Guan Zhirui, Guo Jieying (also known as Yifei), and Wu Huizhen. It is also heard that Yang Naikang, the chief of the second section of the Department of Education, has recommended Song Daodun, Lin Yaqin, and a certain Shan, and Yang Yuangui, commissioned by the Department, has recommended his younger brother to assist in the school. It is expected that the academic atmosphere will improve and the school affairs will be refreshed.

Local News

The City's Elementary School Graduates Will Take a Make-Up Exam on a Set Date 78

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education this year held the elementary school graduation exam. More than five hundred students failed. For the sake of students who failed to pass to continue their studies, the Bureau of Education formulated a procedure and appointed specialized personnel to hold a make-up exam on August 1. There will be two testing grounds, one in Hunan and one in Zhabei. The one in Hunan is located at the Municipal Shihua Elementary School, to be administered by Ge Hongjun, and the one in Zhabei is located at the Municipal Shuji Elementary School, to be administered by Tang Jingxiu. The examinees who have not passed are expected to go to the assigned sites on that day to take the test.

Temporary Registration Oral Examination Time for Elementary School Teachers 79

The method for temporary registration of elementary school teachers in this city has been published in previous reports. Regarding item four, the oral examination, the Municipal Education Bureau has now decided to hold it at the Bureau every Wednesday and Saturday afternoon. Those who have completed the registration procedures and wish to take the oral examination should arrive on time.

Opening of School Supplies Exhibition 80

The School Supplies Exhibition of the Municipal Education Bureau officially opened at 8:30 AM today (the 22nd) at the Xicheng and Meixi school sites. Office hours are from 8:30 AM to 12:00 PM and 1:00 PM to 4:00 PM daily. School supplies from various schools will be delivered for display and arrangement today and tomorrow. It is said that late submissions will not be accepted.

County Education Bureau Adds Central Elementary Schools 81

The Shanghai County Education Bureau, in consideration of the fact that there is only one central elementary school in Minhang, which is also a pilot program, and that no new schools were added in the 18th year due to funding limitations, has decided to designate the Second School as the central school district for each area this year. Tangwan Elementary School will be responsible for the pilot program. A decision will be made after results are seen.
