Global Student Association Recruits Talented Individuals 83

News from the Career Services Department of the Global Chinese Student Association at 95 Carter Road states that there have been numerous requests for specialized personnel recently. A summary is as follows: (1) A certain commercial vocational school in Shanxi seeks a faculty member for the Department of Transportation to teach railway management, transportation, and other commercial subjects. The candidate must prepare their own teaching materials, teach 14 to 18 hours per week, and receive a monthly salary of 140 yuan or more, with accommodation provided but not meals. Travel expenses will be reimbursed. University or vocational school graduates are qualified, and those with experience in the railway industry are particularly suitable. (2) A school in the city has entrusted the association to find a high school normal school or normal university graduate with teaching experience and certification as a Party principles instructor. The monthly salary is generous. Those willing to apply should bring their credentials and examples of their work to the association for an interview as soon as possible.

Second Day of the National Vocational Education Conference 84

Yesterday was the second day of the 10th Annual Meeting of the China Vocational Education Society and the 7th Annual Meeting of the National Federation of Vocational Education Organizations. The details are recorded below:

(I) Vocational Guidance Group Meeting 85

The Vocational Guidance Group (Group Four) meeting was held yesterday at 8:00 AM. Attendees included Zhong Daozan, Zheng Tonghe, Wang Diancun, Shen Youqian, Pan Yangyao, Fan Baohua, Yang Zhefu, Zhang Ying, Yang Xishi, Chao Sun Dingchen, Chen Bokui, Zheng Chunian, Huang Jingwan, Chen Qingshi, Li Banghe, Li Wen Yue, Wang Tianmin, Liao Nancai, Li Xiaobai, Xu Shouqian, Wang Wenbin of the Wu County Vocational Guidance Center, and Lu Linxun of the Jiading Vocational Guidance Center. The meeting was chaired by Wang Diancun. Attendees successively reported on their progress and raised difficulties.

Reports 86

Pan Yangyao (Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center): The Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center was established in September of the 16th year. At that time, the affairs were quite simple, but the work has become increasingly tight to this day. Vocational counseling is especially prevalent, averaging 40 people per day. In addition to services and guidance for further education and employment, attention must also be paid to health and legal aspects. Therefore, health and legal guidance have been recently added. As for vocational placement, statistics show that 300 people register each month, and one-tenth are successfully placed. Moreover, there are many schools in Shanghai with business-like qualities and unscrupulous correspondence schools, so a guide to further education has been compiled to serve as a compass. This is a review of the opening of our organization. Furthermore, the education and vocational sectors have been out of touch for several years, so most institutions and companies do not like to use vocational school graduates. Now, various agencies have gradually gained faith in graduates above the secondary level. Recently, central departments and construction agencies in various localities, as well as banks, factories, and shops, have entrusted our organization to find vocational school graduates, especially engineering students, which is the most needed. Since our establishment, Nanjing, Jiading, Wuxi, and Wu County have also successively organized, gradually drawing the attention of the community. The current trend in the vocational sector should pay attention to industry, so we vigorously promote the study of industry to students to prepare them for local needs. In the future, vocational guidance intends to pay attention to psychological testing, vocational analysis, and aptitude and interests, which is currently being researched and carried out.

Dr. Zhong Daozan: Vocational guidance is of great importance to the future of young people. Due to political circumstances, the Fujian Vocational Guidance Center has not been able to fully implement its set policies, but it is gratifying that it is gradually rising up everywhere.

Fan Baohua (University of Shanghai): The purpose of vocational guidance at our school is twofold: (1) University students do not know which department is suitable when they first enter the school, and they do not know how to serve after graduation. In view of this, our school has listed vocational guidance as a compulsory subject (half a year). This course is designed for first-year university students and is taught by President Liu every week for one hour. On the one hand, it provides theoretical and experiential teaching, and on the other hand, it leads students to visit industrial organizations for reference. In addition, classroom work is not very practical, so a vocational guidance department is set up to bring society and schools closer together. Since the students' circumstances and personalities are different, if guidance is not given, graduates often work in agencies that do not match their studies, and students who have not graduated often feel that they lack interest in what they are learning. Therefore, in addition to contacting various agencies to inquire about students, my brother and President Liu must gather students for discussion for one hour every week. This method has been tested for two years and is very interesting. Therefore, I believe that vocational guidance is very important and should be included in the curriculum so that students will not go astray in the future.

Dr. Shen Gongjian: Vocational guidance should first focus on psychological testing, so attention should be paid to students' interests, environment, and habits. We hope that in the future, scientific methods will be used to make the theory and practice consistent, such as filling out forms and talking. This matter is difficult to see results in a short time, but it will eventually achieve its purpose. American testing can be used as a standard.

Zhang Xiongfei (Jiaxing County Commercial School): The Vocational Placement Committee of our school has been established for a year, but the results are not good. One reason is that the local community does not have confidence in junior high school graduates, and the other reason is that junior high school graduates do not bother to learn business. It is now planned to contact the business community so that graduates can intern in stores for one month before graduation.

Wang Tianmin (Shaanxi Xiyuan Vocational School): Our school has compiled guides to further education

Zheng Xigu (Principal of Shanghai Middle School): Our school handles vocational guidance in two ways: internal and external. (1) The school organizes a guidance department. There are three points of guidance: A. Academic Guidance; B. Guidance for Further Education or Employment; C. Service Guidance. The spirit of teacher-student cooperation is very good. (2) The external level is quite difficult because teachers are busy, especially in Shanghai. For example, I am too busy to respond to entrustments and those who entrust, which wastes a lot of time. I think it is appropriate to set up more vocational guidance centers so that the various guidance centers can jointly handle affairs to ensure that the supplier and the demander benefit each other. After finishing the report, the chairman said that old habits are deeply rooted in the interior. Even if the graduates in the school have good results, it is useless. If the school caters to society, it will fail, but if it is not compatible, it will also fail. Therefore, the chairman advocates creating or improving occupations and asks the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center to be the guide for vocational guidance centers in various places.

Zhang Yingchao (Shengtze Qunyu Pavilion): I have been running the Qunyu Pavilion in Shengtze for many years and have set up a library, museum, and after-work entertainment department to give young people in the business community the opportunity to study. In recent years, various bad habits in Shanghai have been almost completely transferred to the mainland business community, resulting in more and more unemployed people. It is now planned to run a vocational guidance center to provide relief.

Cai Yuanpei, Chairman of the Two Vocational Education Organizations, Delivers the Opening Speech (Cen Hengqing Photo) 87

Chen Bokui (Shanghai Library): When Zheng Ren was running the Library Association, someone asked if the organization and equipment had been trained to run it. I think that running a vocational school in the near future is one of the new occupations.

Zheng Chunian (West District Elementary School): To solve the difficulties of vocational guidance: (1) arouse interest with testing methods; (2) the school must bear the responsibility of transforming society.

Xu Shouqian (Nanjing Vocational Guidance Center): Advocates opening vocational guidance personnel training schools and short-term training courses.

Lu Linxun (Jiading Vocational Guidance Center): During the summer vacation, he went to 15 elementary schools to guide 302 children and found that more people went to further education than employment, more people went to ordinary schools than vocational schools, and more people learned business than engineering. I strongly advocate guiding children to learn direct production industry.

Li Wenbai (Shaanxi Vocational School): Vocational guidance should be trained according to local conditions and time, and should not cater to students' preferences.

Discussion Proposals 88

(1) Proposal to organize a joint vocational guidance organization (submitted by the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center). It was resolved to pass the original proposal. It was assumed that the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center would draft the charter and schedule a conference of various vocational guidance organizations.

(2) Proposal to promote library vocational guidance (Shanghai Library Association). It was resolved to amend and pass the original proposal.

(3) Proposal to promote guidance based on test results (Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center). It was resolved to pass the original proposal. It was recommended that Wang Diancun, Chen Qingshi, Pan Yangyao, Xu Shouqian, and Li Banghe be added to sort out and summarize the following methods: (1) Education administrative agencies in various provinces, cities, and counties should establish vocational guidance personnel training institutes to train vocational guidance talents. (2) Universities, schools, and high schools should establish vocational guidance departments or vocational guidance committees. In addition to experts, leaders from the industry should be invited to join the guidance to facilitate consultation and assistance. (3) Elementary schools should pay attention to guidance for further education and career selection. The local education bureau or vocational guidance center should send experienced personnel to each school to implement guidance and accurately compile statistics. (4) Vocational guidance centers in various places should open more vocational skills training classes according to local needs to train specialized talents. After graduation, the center will be responsible for introducing services so that all sectors can use their talents. In the future, there will be a firm belief in the people introduced by the vocational guidance center. (5) Methods of communication between the education sector and the vocational sector: (A) The education sector should train more specialized talents and cultivate students' moral character and good habits to supply the vocational sector so that it has deep trust and welcome for the students introduced by the vocational guidance center. (B) The education sector should study and improve the academic contribution of agriculture, industry, and commerce to the vocational sector, support the progress of its business, connect feelings, and help each other (such as improving the silk industry, rescuing gold and silver, and improving agricultural production, etc.). (6) Vocational analysis is the basis for the implementation of vocational guidance. Local vocational guidance agencies should conduct a practical survey of local occupations and compile reports to facilitate the process. (7) Experts should be gathered to study vocational psychological testing and compile various vocational testing materials as a basis for implementing vocational guidance. (8) Vocational guidance centers should provide timely assistance and guidance to various needs in the business community. If they obtain their feelings, candidates, interns, and staff will definitely come to entrust them to handle the matter.

(II) Agricultural Education and Rural Education Group 89

The Agricultural Education and Rural Education Group (Group Two) held a meeting. More than 30 attendees included Huang Qisheng, Yao Huiquan, Huang Renzhi, Huai Boming, Song Longtian, Yin Qingtang, Zhang Luquan, Zhang Yuanzhang, Xu Kaiyuan, Zhou Mingyi, Xu Jingren, Shi Jiali, Sun Fang, Cao Fengxiang, Yao Minghui, Fan Yin Shen, Wu Wenkui, Jin Baocheng, Shen Tingfang, Shen Suwen, Shen Xinqing, Liao Jianan, Wang Lin, etc. The meeting was chaired by Zhang Luquan and recorded by Gu Junquan. First, the chairman reported that there were four proposals for this group. Please discuss them in order.

(1) Revise the implementation standards of the rural improvement experimental implementation plan based on several years of experience (proposed by the China Vocational Education Society). The chairman explained that the draft standard was originally formulated by the China Vocational Education Society. Now it is revised based on experience and submitted to this meeting for discussion. The content is very detailed, with a total of 15 items. Now we can discuss them one by one. The public agreed and began to read the first article. Then Huang Renzhi reported on the origin and process of formulating the draft. The conclusion was that we believe that it is impossible to talk about education if we leave the countryside. We must improve it based on its environment and needs, etc. Huang Qisheng thought that the phrase "education as a means" in item 6 A was inappropriate and advocated modification. Huang Renzhi agreed and explained the work that should be done in the countryside, such as light-interest lending, medicine, and medical treatment, etc., all of which must be based on livelihood. Huang Qisheng, the director, changed the item to "Start with education, with farmers as the main body and livelihood as the center." Shen Suwen advocated deleting the word "education." Yao Huiquan advocated that the word "education" must be retained and the word "means" can be modified appropriately, and explained that the so-called education is broad. Our society advocates the unity of wealth and education, so we should implement education in all aspects to increase the knowledge of the rural people and relieve their suffering, etc. Huang Renzhi agreed and proposed specific amendments to the article "All improvement undertakings are centered on education, and assisting in solving livelihood problems is the starting method," and explained that education is everywhere and must be absolutely linked to life. On the one hand, improvement undertakings solve the livelihood problems of each villager, and on the other hand, they still need to solve the public economy of the village. We should not create a beautiful environment for the village, plant flowers and plants, and use music to make it colorful, and then compile simple songs so that everyone can easily learn to sing, so that young children can cultivate their character in this environment and be qualified to be villagers and citizens in the future, etc. The whole body agreed to pass the amendment. Huang Qisheng, the main deletion of the word "Anping" in the seventh article Anle and Qin Anping Yao Huiquan explained that Kang Le and Qin refer to spiritual Anping, which is not the same as the formal meaning. Huang Renzhi and Shen Xinqing "advocated that there is no need to modify it. The chairman paid for the vote, and the result was not modified. Shen Xinqing, the main deletion of the three words "front line" in Item C, Fourth Item of Article 9. The whole body agreed. In Article 9, Item A, Tenth Item, the two words "but to" were changed to the word "such as." All other articles were passed according to the original draft without any objections. It was also discussed that the whole case would be submitted to the plenary meeting for discussion tomorrow morning. Secondly, the chairman proposed that members introduce each other. Everyone agreed that each person would register on their own and briefly describe their resume. Later, the chairman introduced Zhou Mingyi to give a speech on the situation of the Suiyuan New Agricultural Experimental Site. The words are omitted. The rest (2) Proposal to improve rural education (proposed by Lu Shaoji) Yao Huiquan mainly handed over the matter to the Vocational Education Society for reference. The chairman voted, and it was passed without objection. (3) Please add a sales office for high-quality seeds to your society (proposed by Biao Boming). Yao Huiming explained that in addition to the new agricultural tool promotion office, the society's rural service department has also started to promote high-quality seeds. It seems that this proposal does not need to be established. The chairman voted, and it was passed without objection. (4) Proposal to establish a new agricultural trial and rental office (proposed by Lin Anbang) Yao Huiquan explained that the China Vocational Education Society's new agricultural tool promotion office originally had trial and rental methods. The trial has now been implemented, and the rental has been temporarily suspended due to practical difficulties. Is there a solution? Please submit it to the conference for discussion. The chairman paid for the vote and it was passed.

(III) Industrial and Commercial Education Group Meeting 90

Attendees: Yang Weiyu, Meng Xiyan, Wang Zhongxiang, Zhu Fangshi, Zhang Zulie, Liao Zuyin, Zhao Ziyi, Yang Peiwen, Zhao Shifu, Wan Sinian. Chairman: Zhao Shifu. The following proposals were discussed: (1) In order to restore rights and interests, resist imported goods, and develop my country's industry and commerce, we should vigorously promote arts and crafts education and establish specialized schools to cultivate talents. It was resolved in principle to pass the proposal and hand it over to the China Vocational Education Society to supplement opinions and submit it to the Ministry of Education for consideration. (2) Pay attention to commercial education. It was resolved that this proposal could be sent to commercial high schools and university business schools for reference. At the same time, it was submitted to the Ministry of Finance and Industry and Commerce to issue a notice to all financial and industrial and commercial agencies across the country to uniformly adopt new-style bookkeeping. At the same time, we should also send a letter to the chambers of commerce in various provinces to advise them, and during the initial commercial study period in schools, we can also study old-style bookkeeping to assist in reference. (3) Implement labor education. It was resolved to ask the China Vocational Education Society to formulate detailed methods and contact the factory, and at the same time submit it to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to issue a notice to all factories to pay attention to labor education. (4) The teaching materials of workers' schools should be compiled separately according to the occupational nature of their students. It was resolved to ask the China Vocational Education Society to promote the main purpose of this proposal to various industrial combinations and agencies separately. (5) Please ask the government to stipulate the method of collecting factory school funding donations and issue a notice to all factories across the country to comply with it. It was resolved to retain this proposal. (6) Promote popular vocational supplementary education. It was resolved to ask the China Vocational Education Society to formulate detailed methods according to the removal of items 3 and 5 and submit them separately. (7) Implement supplementary education and establish libraries. It was resolved to send a letter to the Library Association for consideration and implementation. At the same time, Aizhi vocational schools should expand vocational libraries and submit a request to the Ministry of Education to order provinces and counties to establish vocational libraries. (8) Organize a work-study education committee to study and investigate work-study plans as a contribution to the implementation of a part of work-study in the domestic Central University. It was resolved to ask the China Vocational Education Society to handle it with reference to this proposal. (9) The society should raise funds to set up a bank to support the development of small-scale agricultural, industrial, and commercial industries, so as to increase the number of occupational positions and the amount of production and benefit the society. It was resolved to ask the China Vocational Education Society to consult with economic experts and industrialists who are enthusiastic about this cause to study methods and earnestly promote it. (10) Establish a large-scale correspondence university to facilitate the universality of higher education. It was resolved to temporarily retain it.

(IV) Welcoming Conference of 17 Organizations 91

At 6:00 PM, at the invitation of 17 organizations including the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, Daxia University, Tongji University, China Arts and Crafts Society, China Science Society, Chinese Institute of Engineers, Shanghai Machinery Association, Fudan University, Guanghua University, China Enamel Factory, Datong Bookstore, Zhonghua Book Company, University of Shanghai, Commercial Press, China Iron Factory, and China Vocational School, a welcoming banquet was held at the New World Restaurant.

(V) Today's Second Plenary Meeting 92

The second plenary meeting was held in the assembly hall of the Society at 9:00 AM today. The agenda was as follows: (1) Open the meeting and perform the ceremony as usual; (2) Report on the resolutions of the first plenary meeting and group meetings; (3) Discussion: (A) Mr. Zhong Zhixiu's opinions on the conference; (B) Location of the next Vocational Education Organization Joint Conference and the chairman of the year; (C) Other (4) Closing.

(6) Zhong Zhixiu's Opinions on the Conference 93

(1) In the past annual meetings, many proposals were put forward and resolved, but few were implemented. It would be better to change to discussing problems, that is, to submit the most difficult or most rewarding points felt by the schools in the past two years for discussion, or to criticize them, so that other schools can adopt them. This can avoid bureaucratic meetings and only get a few dead resolutions. (Private organizations have no political power to speak of, it is better to provide the results of the discussion for people to adopt.) (2) Six months before each meeting or at the end of each meeting, jointly decide on the central issues for the next or current meeting, such as moral education liaison, educational methods, graduate prospects and supplementary studies. Designate several experts in advance to prepare the discussion topics, scope and procedures so that members can prepare in advance for purposeful participation, so that one case will not be raised by A, and another case will be raised by B, so that all proposals cannot be discussed with prepared and sufficient materials. (3) Each vocational school does not have a concise report and lacks a research attitude of contact, which can be used as a basis for improvement. The General Assembly should prepare a report format in advance and ask them to fill it out. It is not necessary for each school to report at the meeting, just choose the main points to report. Moreover, it can be based on this report to make a general report for the reference of the world.

(7) Exhibition Welcomes Visitors 94

The society is holding an exhibition this time to provide the public with a view of the achievements of vocational education. The exhibits include the society's books, charts, statistics, vocational guidance, statistics of entrusted projects introduced in talks, and psychological testing equipment. The financial, educational, agronomic, Youan construction, and entertainment facilities of the Xugongqiao Huangxu Township Rural Improvement Association are all made into drawings. Dozens of Central University's College of Agriculture, Jinling University's Department of Agriculture's cotton, wheat, rice, fruit tree, silkworm breeding specimens, and planting tool charts and descriptions. The achievements of the China Vocational School, the China New Agricultural Implements Promotion Institute, the China Iron Factory, the China Enamel Factory, the Zhejiang Jiangsu Zhenjiang Women's Vocational School, etc., are no less than thousands of pieces. It is open as usual today, and all sectors are welcome to visit.

The Chinese Expeditionary Football Team Arrives in Singapore 95

Hu Wenhu Hosts, Practices and Prepares for Battle

(Singapore Correspondence, July 11) The Chinese Expeditionary Football Team arrived in Singapore on the 9th. The previous communication has been noted. Now, the situation after arriving at the port is described as follows:

Hu Wenhu Provides Food and Accommodation The team of thirteen people was led by Hu Wenhu's representative, Hu Guigeng, to several specially prepared cars, which sped away to Hu Wenhu's villa in Pasir Panjang. Since Hu received the radio sent by the team from the wheel, he ordered people to prepare everything. The food, accommodation, etc. in the villa have been properly arranged. The Chinese athletes will be able to safely stay here for a few days. The cost of food, accommodation, and travel for the team in Singapore will also be fully provided by Hu Wenhu, as it was when the South Expedition team came last year.

The Chinese Team Prepares for Battle The first opponent of the Chinese team will be the Malaysian Chinese United Team, the leader of the Malaysian football world. The team recently defeated the South China team, which is known for its strength, by a score of 3-1. This time, in addition to the original Lok Wah players, the Chinese team has also added several famous South China players, Cao Guicheng and Chen Guangyao. With a wealth of talent, they have a grand ambition to dominate the Malay Peninsula. However, the opponent is indeed a strong enemy that is not easy to defeat, so they have been practicing hard to prepare for the battle. The lineup against the Malaysian Chinese United Team on the 13th is tentatively set as follows:

Chen Guangyao

To Be Dismissed with a Smile 99

Husband (His wife sneaks up from behind. Suddenly kisses him)丨Eh. We've been married for several years. Why are you still like when you were in love with me at the beginning?

Wife丨Oh my. Sorry. I mistook someone. Why is it you sitting here?

Theater Usher (Speaking to a woman who fell from the moon tower)丨Madam. Have you been hurt in any way by this fall?

Woman丨Nothing else, the biggest injury. is losing one of the best seats in the moon tower, really a pity.

A丨The style of your hat is very good. How much did you pay for it?

B丨Did not pay. Because the clerk in that hat shop. happened not to be at the counter.

A丨You entrusted her husband to deliver the love letter to her. Isn't it too presumptuous? Aren't you afraid that he will open it secretly?

B丨No no. Because I wrote on the letter. "Enclosed is a love letter. Others must not open it secretly."

A丨Could you possibly lend me ten dollars?

B丨I don't know you. How can I bear to part with money.

A丨It's because the people I know are unwilling to lend me. So I have to borrow from strangers.

A Painting Visit to Linggu Notes, Peng Zhou 100

Recently went to the capital. I heard that my old friend Liang Dingming built a painting studio in Yang of Linggu Temple. He will make a large oil painting as a wall decoration for the Memorial Hall of the Martyrs Cemetery. Liang is from Guangdong. He is good at oil painting, charcoal, etc. He works in the Whampoa Military Academy and the Central Party Department. His paintings are full of revolutionary spirit. Therefore, he is called a revolutionary painter by the people of the time. Some time ago, he went to Europe to study fine arts on the order of Chairman Chiang. After returning to China, it happened that the central government proposed to build a martyrs' cemetery, and there was a preparatory committee. The chairman was Chiang Chung-cheng. The members were He Yingqin, etc. The secretary was Chen Guofu. The architect was a Westerner, Murphy. The engineer was Liu Mengxi. And the art item. Then Liang Jun is in charge. A preparatory office has been set up in Linggu Temple. The budget is 500,000 yuan. It will take three years to complete.

On Sunday, I drove to visit Liang Jun. When I arrived at the temple, I saw that Zhang Jingyu, Zhang Zhihan, and He Yushu were having fun taking pictures with Liang Jun. Seeing me arrive. Happily said goodbye. After Zhang and others left. I then accompanied Liang Jun into the room for a talk. Asked about the painting situation. Liang Jun told me. This move is really one of the greatest creations of my life. I will devote my energy to it. I am currently searching for painting materials. To describe the revolutionary history. On the one hand, looking for craftsmen to select materials. Build a large painting studio that is 26 feet high and 42 feet long. On one side, 6,000 yuan of canvas and 15,000 yuan of oil paints have been ordered from abroad. When they arrive. I will use three years of dedicated effort to create this mural that is 20 feet high and 400 feet in circumference. After the painting is successful. According to Chairman Chiang's intention, a special hall will be built to display it. Ordinary buildings are not suitable. It is estimated that work will begin in five months. The red sun is in the mountains. I said goodbye. Go back and remember it. To tell those who visit Linggu for paintings.

Peach and Lotus Yang Yixiao 102

Every summer. I always remember the Shanghai yellow mud wall honey peach. And the Yuyuan Siamese lotus. Looking back on the vicissitudes of life. It's only been twenty or thirty years. It makes people feel the past and present.

The most famous is the yellow mud wall honey peach. When the peaches are ripe. You can go inside to buy and eat your fill. However, people are not allowed to take a peach out. I'm afraid to keep the pits for private planting. Later, because the houses were renovated. The peach trees are no longer there.

Yuyuan used to have Siamese lotus flowers. It was very prosperous for a while. Later, the lotus flowers in the pond gradually deteriorated. Now there is only a lotus pond. And there are no lotus flowers to see. Re-do it to make up for the regret. Unexpectedly, Mr. was plagued by illness. The disease never recovered. He can no longer engage in painting. Then how can Xin Hange's owner expect it? Mr. is good at calligraphy. It resembles Nuan Sou. In the past, he taught at the Wuzhong Caoqiao School. Students always asked for calligraphy couplets. Mr. complained about it. It is not difficult to write, but it is difficult to grind ink. The students then stored ink in urns. Asking for it never stops. Mr. was even more distressed. Then he posted a price list to refuse. And the annoyance began to resolve. The Northern Expedition was successful. Mr. took a job at the Wuzhong Water Police Political Training Department. During the leisure time of documents, he still sold calligraphy for wine money. His declaration is very elegant. Such as cloud. Tiansui is in distress and determined. For more than ten years. Only supported by pen and ink. Now I am lucky that Chong'er has restored the country. Lu and Jie Tui. Official hidden in Wumen. Willing to be a soldier. Even though the name is cheap. It has been revealed in newspapers. Old friends and new acquaintances. I am annoyed by pen and ink. I don't know to serve the public. Equal to hiring. Since politics is a job. It is not as leisurely as a yamen. After the documents are processed. The shape and spirit have been exhausted. I also think about my old business. Nourish my nature. However, due to the limitation of energy. It is difficult to apply to everyone. Therefore, I seek enlightenment. Think of getting a little bit of moisture. The crane salary is thin, so I can support honesty. Jia Hui will be issued first. I must be quick to obey the order. Send feelings to calligraphy. Fortunately, there is no suspicion of selling goods. Conclude a contract with lichen. If there is a habit of being obsessed. It resembles the essays of the Six Dynasties. It makes people chew endlessly. In addition to poetry and ancient prose, Mr. is also good at epigraphy, medicine, and Buddhist studies. I once said to Bu Xun. If you have leisure time. If each art can be pondered for several more years. All can be famous families. But trapped by life. Busy all day long. Spirit is not good. It's hateful. My son is studying at Chengzhong Middle School. In his spare time, he likes to write novels. It is very simple, Yongyou is interesting. It is truly a promising material.

Lingering Garden Summer Notes, Cheng Zhizheng, sent from Suzhou 103

The red emperor is rampant. The heat is like roasting. Living in Shanghai. Heard and witnessed. Apart from the hustle and bustle. There are very few ways to escape the heat. In early July. I was assigned to a short-term internship on the Beijing-Shanghai Road. Details in the station. The station chief, Mr. Xu Yonggui, gave instructions one by one. I have a lot of experience. In the afternoon, I proposed to visit Lingering Garden. I have heard the name of Lingering Garden for a long time. I have been running around in the secular world. Since last year. I wanted to go there but failed. Now I have fulfilled my long-cherished wish. The joy can be known. Enter the door. I and my colleagues used the name of the internship group. Ask for free admission. The gatekeeper did not allow it. After persisting for a long time. Change to half price. A little further in. I saw lush green shade. Winding paths. Enter a large hall. There is a pool in front of the hall. Shaded by lush trees. The pool water is dark green as if dyed. There are many goldfish in it. I bought some cakes and fed them. The fish scrambled for food. Stirring the water into a huge vortex. A friend brought a fast lens. Take a photo as a souvenir. The hall faces a rockery. The mountain is stacked with interesting features. Or rise like a cliff. Or stand precariously like a jagged rock. Mixed among the rocks. Most of them are ancient trees. Branching branches and trunks. Standing like ghosts and demons. The mountain wind blows. I don't know where I am. Rest for a while. Climb up the steps. A pavilion every five steps. A pavilion every ten steps. The exquisite architecture. The secluded arrangement. Sigh. Turn right. Enter the East Garden. It contains a complete set of books and illustrations. There are glass trees in it. But it has been sealed. I haven't had a chance to read it yet. In the hall. There is a huge plaque of the imperial calligraphy Lin Quan Qi Shuo. Golden and brilliant. Dazzling. It is said that it was handwritten by Emperor Qianlong. The gate is Dongshan silk and bamboo. The key is down. I heard there was a dance pavilion inside. Today, the gate is deserted. Desolate and unbearable. There are many stalagmites in front of the Guanyun Building. The place is also quiet. Going further from "Another Village". Go around a big circle in the garden. Climb to Zhile Pavilion. The pavilion is on the top of the mountain. Host

The supervisor briefly inquired about the luggage brought in. Then he signed each one to exempt from inspection and release. The Immigration Bureau Commissioner said. I came to the ship to take care of it. To avoid difficulties at the station. But I only need to see Mr. Mei's face. Then shake hands. In Japan, he was already famous several years ago. This time in the United States. And received great welcome. And most of the residents here are from these three countries. Then Mr. Mei's arrival here. It should be the most welcomed person here in several years. After talking for a long time. Sweet Warmth in My Heart (338) by Bao Tianxiao 105

Chapter Thirteen: Who Unintentionally Sowed Blessings and Obtained a Closed Circle, Only This Predestined Relationship Has the Heart to Sing "Golden Threads"

Let's talk about Zuo Shichen and Long Ziyun...sitting on the grass of Wei Chun Garden, sipping tea. They gradually felt the night deepening... many gentlemen and ladies enjoying the cool breeze came. Because they heard that there would be fireworks at eleven o'clock tonight... everyone wanted to join the excitement. In fact, the so-called Eastern fireworks... are very simple... similar to our Chinese shooting star firecrackers... but they can emit red and green colors. The original Dongguan fireworks in China... can conjure up various stories... such as Emperor Xuanzong of Tang visiting the Moon Palace, the Cowherd and Weaver Girl meeting on the Magpie Bridge, etc. Today there are both Chinese and foreign fireworks... which is even more of a sensation for a while... Amidst laughter... a gust of evening wind passed by... carrying the scent of jasmine flowers on the temples... and the fragrance of white orchids on the chest... particularly elegant and charming. Zuo Shichen even wanted to meet Ruiyun, whom he hadn't seen for a long time, here... Although many colorful electric lights were installed on the grass in the bushes... in order to attract coolness, there was not much bright light. Just as Zuo Shichen turned his head, he saw Ruiyun avoiding his gaze... and talking and laughing with a female companion. Zuo Shichen thought that Ruiyun had not seen him... so he said softly to Long Ziyun... Mr. Long... it really is Ruiyun. But she didn't see me... look, isn't she talking to someone? Long Ziyun smiled... She saw you a long time ago... before you turned your head. She had already been looking at you... but she only saw your back silhouette... she was still wondering if it was you or not... Although she also recognized me a little... When you turned your head, she naturally confirmed that it was you... Probably a courtesan who has married into a respectable family... all the things from the past... seem to have died. As the ancients said... "All past things... are like yesterday's death... all future things... are like today's birth"... This can be regarded as a footnote to a prostitute's marriage into a respectable family... After marrying someone... it's like changing a lifetime. All the things from the past in the brothel... can only be regarded as things from a previous life. The guests who were known in the brothel in the past... can only be regarded as people from a previous life... People from a previous life... and people from this life... are completely unrelated. Have you ever seen people from this life... still recognizing people from a previous life? Zuo Shichen also agreed with Long Ziyun... but he said... This can really be regarded as "a world away"... But this "a world away"... is a man-made separation... not a natural separation... Although she is already a person of this world... I still recognize her after all... and she still recognizes me... it's just that we don't greet each other... Long Ziyun said... Naturally, we can't greet each other... She has many female companions here now... If she greets a strange man... gossip will immediately arise... I saw that when you turned your head, she avoided your gaze... When you didn't look at her, she was secretly looking at you... You didn't see it... but I saw it very clearly...

Fluctuations in Gold Bar Quotations Show Uncertainty 106

Market conditions are intricate and confusing, seemingly pointing to an upward trend. Yesterday, the 21st, gold bar quotations showed uncertainty, with frequent rises and falls. The morning session saw fluctuations of about six taels of silver, and the afternoon session saw a change of four taels, but with an underlying upward trend. Exchange rates rose suddenly by half a point, but internally remained flat. Banks sold off slightly, but trading within the market remained broad. Firms such as Fuchang, Hengxing, and Wanxing all made purchases, while Yuansheng, Yuchang, and Shengyong showed strong selling intentions, but all firms lacked a clear direction, resulting in confusion and uncertainty. From the morning, with little movement on major transactions, the market opened high, with many buyers still present. A peak was subsequently observed, but the availability of drafts seemed limited, and with Yuansheng and others selling off, the price once fell by five or six taels, plunging to 92.5 taels. However, with eager buying, the price quickly rose by five taels. Later in the session, Fuchang, Hengxing, Yuancheng, and Yong and others continued to buy, while Yuansheng, Yuxing, Yong, Wanxing, and others all sold off positions, giving the market an appearance of strength, although with occasional fluctuations of two or three taels. With the draft market stabilizing, the price closed above 597 taels. As yesterday was a Monday, there was no major cable report, but Sunday's telegraphic dispatches showed no expansion or contraction. American banks increased by one-eighth.

The morning market was bumpy, with the September opening at 598 taels, up 1.8 taels. Gross prices fluctuated by two or three taels, lingering around 97 taels. Exchange rates remained flat. Mitsui sold near-term Japanese gold at 1 tael, 3 mace, 3 fen, 8 li, 7 hao, 5 si, and Dalian gold at 1 tael, 3 mace, 4 fen, 2 li, 5 hao. Subsequently, the price moved from 96.23 taels to 98.89 taels, with Xianling announcing a rise of 1.25, US dollars up 2.5 jiao, and Japanese gold down 1 fen, trading at 97.26 to 7.6 taels, fluctuating by six or seven jiao within a few minutes. With internal slackening, near-term Japanese gold was available for sale at 1 tael, 3 mace, 3 fen, 3 li, 7 hao, 5 si, with Zhifeng, Yonghengxing, and hedge traders selling off, causing the price to plummet by five taels to 92.5 taels by 9:50 am. Shortly after, with movements of two, four, or five qian, each party began pursuing purchases after 10:15 am, causing prices to rise sharply by over five taels. However, Xianling and other firms remained stable, with no changes, and fellow traders showed little inflow or outflow. By 11:30 am, the market surged to 98.2 taels, then fell back by one tael in an instant, with fluctuations around seven taels. The market closed at 97.7 taels at noon.

The evening market recovered, rising by 1.2 taels. The afternoon market opened at 97.7 taels, then rose by over one tael to 99.1 taels, with Senchang, Yong, and others buying. Afterward, the market showed a latent state of weakness. HSBC sold August British gold at 6 pence, 1 li, 8 hao, 7 si, 5 hu, and Taiwan sold Japanese gold at 1 tael, 3 mace, 3 fen, 7 li, 5 hao. Yuansheng and others sold off, causing the price to fall to 96.6 taels by 2:45 pm. Subsequently, with Fuchang and Hengxing buying, the price rose again by two taels, reaching 98.6 taels by 3:45 pm. Suddenly, news arrived that the Indian exchange rate had risen again in the Three Kingdoms over the weekend. Sellers immediately became active, causing the price to drop by 3.5 taels to 95 taels. At 4:00 pm, Hengxing made a large bid, causing the price to jump by over three taels to 98.7 taels. By the 4:30 pm close, the market was at 97.4 taels, a rise of 1.2 taels compared to the previous weekend (the 19th), reversing the decline of the previous two or three days.

The listed price is still suppressed by over 50 taels. The highest price of the day was 99.1 taels, and the lowest price was 92.5 taels, a range of 6.6 taels. The listed price has been revised to 652.2 taels, with Japanese gold listed at a decrease of 1 fen. The morning market saw suppression of 54 or 55 taels, then around 60 taels. At noon, the suppression was down to about 54 taels. In the early afternoon, the suppression was down to 53 or 54 taels, then estimated at 57 taels. The final suppression was still about 55 taels. Goods opened at 8.4 qian in the morning, closed at 7.7 qian at noon, and 7.5 qian in the afternoon and at the close.

Hedge traders come and go. British Silver Dollars No Longer Trade at a Premium 109

In recent months, the availability of ready silver dollars in Hong Kong has been insufficient for circulation. Furthermore, the Hong Kong exchange rate is higher than the Shanghai exchange rate. Consequently, British silver dollars have been used as a substitute for Hong Kong silver dollars. Thus, the market price of British silver dollars in Hong Kong has been the same as that of Hong Kong silver dollars. However, the market price of Hong Kong silver dollars has consistently been over 8 qian and 2 fen, while the purchase of British silver dollars in Shanghai, even with a premium of several fen, has still been worthwhile. As a result, small qianzhuang involved in spot trading have been rushing to purchase them. Consequently, the import of British silver dollars into Hong Kong has been accumulating daily, eventually reaching saturation. However, the inflow has continued uninterrupted. The Hong Kong authorities, fearing changes in the market, have prohibited the import of British silver dollars. Passengers landing are prohibited from carrying more than 50 yuan, and large shipments are completely prohibited. Therefore, the sales channels for British silver dollars have been cut off, and the supply to Shanghai has been unable to continue. As a result, British silver dollars recently have no longer traded at a premium and are treated the same as ordinary silver dollars. The previous premium of 5 or 6 fen per silver dollar is now a distant memory.

Grain Foodstuffs - Eastern New "Jing" Rice Selling Briskly 117

Chen Bai Jing Rice Drops Frequently by More Than Half a Yuan

Zhabei: Yesterday, over ten boats of inland rice arrived. Inventory along the riverbank has gradually thickened. Wholesale sales on this street are slow, and buying sentiment is exceptionally subdued. Changzhou-Wuxi northern "Jing" rice again fell by about twenty coppers yesterday. In the past two days, it has already fallen by a substantial half yuan. Since the Bureau of Social Affairs approved free transactions between rice merchants and rice shops, all evaluation meetings only execute procedures for registering incoming goods. Covert price fixing and private posting of prices have completely disappeared because the rice merchants declared that violation would be fined one thousand yuan. Therefore, daily shop sales are largely stagnant, and transactions are scarce. Currently, factory goods, warehouse goods, boat goods, and other "Bai Jing" rice require special top-grade rice which opens at twenty-one yuan. Medium and inferior grades are uniformly discounted based on quality. Market conditions are gradually returning to their original state, but "Jing" rice prices are rapidly declining. Eastern new "Jing" rice has already been listed for sample viewing. In the past two days, over three hundred "shi" have been seen. The price opens at twenty-one yuan and sells very well. Although this new "Jing" rice is slightly broken, buyers greatly welcome it. If the weather can remain sunny for a long time, the number of shipments will definitely be strong, and the price may be difficult to sustain. Those with flexible capital raise prices to undercut competitors. The general market is mixed with firm and weak prices; top-grade goods still open at about nineteen and a half yuan.

Hu Nan: About ten boats have arrived from the river. Shop sales are flat. Since the Eastern new rice was transacted, people's hearts have been dispirited. Furthermore, foreign rice has also fallen by twenty or thirty coppers. Saigon small-grain rice transactions are becoming scarce, and the price is also softening. The "Jing" rice market is therefore difficult to sustain. Although the price has fallen, sales remain sluggish, and the trend is increasingly weak. General market prices are all at twenty yuan and five or six coppers. Although thin-husked rice goods are not strong, they are also declining along with "Jing" rice. Interest from all parties is lacking. "Le" short-grain rice is permissible, but "Yang Du Jian" rice is not being inquired about. The market price only opens at the nineteen yuan mark, and it requires a change of about half a yuan. Yuan goods are scarce, sales are weak, and market prices are stable, opening high at nineteen.

Foreign Rice Continues to Fall by Half a Yuan 118

Shanghai Inventory at Five Hundred Thousand Bags

Down Two Yuan Compared to the Beginning of Last Week

Yesterday, foreign rice showed fatigue and sluggishness in the morning. Those customers who intended to speculate and hoard were wavering even more, and many did not hesitate to lower prices to sell. There was surplus seeking to be sold, so the situation became more depressed. The price then dropped slightly by about half a yuan. After this drop, local inland cheap-rice hoarders and scattered laborers inquired. The total market transaction volume exceeded ten thousand bags, and the market price was able to stabilize, but it was already down by fifty coppers compared to the previous market and about two yuan for each small-grain and number two Saigon rice compared to the highest market price of last week. Fortunately, the high-grade goods were supported by "Du" rice, and the decline was slower. The rice stored in Shanghai, excluding the inventory handled in this street, is estimated to be about five hundred thousand bags, with high-grade goods accounting for only one or two tenths. Yesterday's sales included one thousand five hundred bags of number one Saigon rice, priced at seventeen yuan and four coppers to seventeen yuan; three hundred bags of Annam rice, priced at seventeen yuan and six coppers; one thousand bags of Qieladi rice, priced at seventeen yuan and three coppers; four thousand bags of small-grain rice, priced at fifteen yuan and four coppers to fourteen yuan and five coppers; two thousand bags of large-grain rice, priced at thirteen yuan and one copper and three fen to twelve yuan and eight coppers; special high-grade rice, priced at thirteen yuan and seven coppers; one thousand bags of small-grain rough rice, priced at eleven yuan and eight coppers; and three hundred bags of Xuye rough rice, priced at thirteen yuan and five coppers.

Furthermore, it is reported that the reason for yesterday's sharp decline in foreign rice is superficially due to the suspension of customer orders and the price reduction by the owners. In reality, it is because the Jianghai Customs Office prohibited the reporting and transportation of foreign wheat to Yingkou and other ports. Customer gangs were unable to load and transport it, and they all sought to sell, causing a significant impact on the market. Medium and inferior goods have a large inventory and are particularly weak. Large-grain rice sold for only twelve yuan and two or three coppers near evening, a decrease of nearly one yuan compared to last weekend. Other small-grain rice decreased by half a yuan to seventy or eighty coppers. However, number one Saigon rice and other high-grade goods have less inventory and are better off.

Flour Sharply Falls by About Thirty Fen 119

Rice Prices Loosen on All Sides, Northern Sales Blocked Entirely

Inland Ejects First, Manufacturers Dump Later

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, all months uniformly fell sharply. The original momentum of the previous rise originated from the soaring rice prices, reaching a historically high price. As a result, the general inland gangs purchased aggressively step by step, leading to intense popular sentiment, and the flour market also surged along with it. Until recently, due to the new rice having already entered the market, rice prices in various places also began to loosen. Coupled with the blockade of northern sales, the actual sales market suffered a major blow. Therefore, the most enthusiastic inland gangs, under the pressure of the environment, have abandoned their prejudices and are gradually selling off in large quantities. Manufacturers are also dumping step by step due to the lack of sales. Therefore, the strength of the selling pressure from the opening to the closing of the market was rare recently. Although the quotation for foreign wheat was four, five, or six coppers better, popular sentiment has already changed and did not prop it up at all. As a result, July and August fell by two fen compared to the previous week's closing price, September fell by three fen and two and a half li, October fell by three and a half fen, November fell by two fen and seven and a half li, and December fell by three fen.

Wheat Prices Plummet by More Than One "Qian" 120

Early Ripening and Bumper Harvest... Flour Sales Stagnant... Large Speculators Dump in Large Quantities

Yesterday, after the opening of the future wheat market in the morning, prices for all months fell sharply. Because the inland gang bulls have gradually sold off, and the local speculators, in view of the sluggish overseas sales and the stagnation of the wheat on the market, turned their attention and dumped in large quantities, especially the major speculators close to a certain factory, whose dumping was the most significant, causing popular sentiment to waver greatly, like a gale sweeping down, with the momentum of a river flowing straight down. Because of the general perception of early ripening and a bumper harvest, and wheat also stagnant due to the poor sales of flour, speculators' sentiments became very strong. It is estimated that the lowest price this month fell to four liang, five qian, and seven fen; August to four liang and six qian, a sharp drop of one qian and a half compared to the previous week; September to four liang and seven qian; October to four liang and seven qian and six fen; November to four liang and eight qian; and December to four liang and six qian and four fen, a drop of one qian or one qian and three or four fen. By the afternoon opening, there was a slight rebound due to short covering, but ultimately, the bearish momentum was still strong, and it showed signs of weakness again. As a result, July, August, September, and October increased by one qian and two fen compared to the previous week, November fell by one qian, and December fell by one qian and one fen. Because the factory still firmly refuses to move the wheat and the standard has already plummeted, the medium-high goods have also decreased by about one qian, while the medium-inferior goods have reached as much as two qian. For example, the inferior Gaoyou wheat opened at only four liang, three qian, and two fen, which shows the fierceness of the falling trend. It is estimated that a total of nine thousand six hundred bags of Gaoyou, Shuikou, Baoying, and Shashi wheat were opened, with Fuxin and Shenda purchasing half of them.

Local News

After the Escalation of the French-Owned Water and Electricity Labor Strike 122

Major Bloodshed on Rue Mâlang Yesterday

Twenty-Four Workers Arrested

More Than Twenty People Shot

Stray Bullet Kills One Innocent Person

Municipal Party Committee Cables Central Government to Protest

The French-owned water and electricity labor strike escalated further yesterday, leading to a major tragedy on Rue Mâlang. The details are compiled as follows:

Cause of the Tragedy: Since the outbreak of the labor strike at the company, it has dragged on for a month, with no hope of resolution. At present, it has almost moved from mediation to despair. Currently, although there are more than two hundred workers from the company's transportation department joining in the assistance, there are still a considerable number of people serving the company as usual. They have been repeatedly advised, recounting the company executives' step-by-step oppressive actions, such as armed detectives riding in cars following each tram that has been dispatched recently, and various demonstrations of strong-arm tactics. However, those who advised were earnest, but ultimately to no avail. This provoked public outrage, and more than two hundred workers from the machinery and transportation departments gathered at the Workers' Club on Rue Mâlang in the French Concession at around 8:00 AM yesterday to question them. Unexpectedly, when the large group of unarmed workers were heading there, the French police had already learned of it, mistakenly believing that they were about to riot, and immediately dispatched a large number of armored vehicles loaded with more than one hundred armed guards and police officers who opened fire and strafed the crowd. The crowd was greatly angered and was forced to retreat, but more than twenty people had already been shot and injured, unable to move, and were all arrested. A stray bullet also killed one innocent person, a mason, whose name is not known.

Conditions of Injuries: Fourteen arrested workers, most of whom were seriously injured and unable to move. It is reported that after the arrest, the police initially detained them in one room and took their statements, then sent the seriously injured to the hospital for treatment. Among the workers who escaped, one was seriously injured and four were slightly injured. One of the seriously injured and one of the slightly injured were sent to Shanghai Hospital for treatment, while the others volunteered to go home for medical treatment.

Purchasing Medications: The French-owned water and electricity union, because the workers were suddenly strafed by the ruthless bullets of the imperialists, with as many as twenty people injured, although a portion had already been arrested, and there was no reliable news regarding treatment, immediately sent personnel to purchase a large batch of medications to try to send to the arrested people and the injured people outside to help them with their treatment. After learning of this, the Chinese tram workers' union also donated a considerable amount of medications.

Conditions of the Transportation Department: The conditions demanded by the transportation department are attached as follows: 1. Public buses, trackless trams, and trams will be assigned shifts in rotation, and all workers, regardless of seniority, will be equal. 2. Routes 6 and 3 must use two people to sell tickets, and large Route 2 buses of the third class must use one person to open doors. 3. Cancel the ringing of the bell to let passengers off, cancel unwarranted penalties and suspensions, and do not fire without cause. 4. Daily work must be eight hours, and overtime pay will be added accordingly. 5. If there is a danger when driving, the company should be responsible, and the driver will not be held responsible in any way. 6. The hiring of people or the suspension of business must be approved by the workers. 7. Three sets of uniform clothing must be issued each year, two sets of lined clothing and three sets of unlined clothing, and one overcoat. Regardless of seniority, all must be issued new clothing. 8. Roll call wages will be paid as usual. 9. Restore the jobs of unemployed workers. 10. It is necessary to recognize the workers' union and have the right to representation. 11. Cancel the club's public expenses and subsidize the union. 12. Each worker will receive an additional eight yuan in wages per month. 13. An annual bonus of two months' wages.

Chinese Employees Join: The company's senior Chinese employees had originally intended to join immediately, as reported in yesterday's newspapers. After yesterday's tragedy, they became even more indignant and resolutely joined together. They elected more than sixty representatives who reported to the French-owned water and electricity union at 4:00 PM yesterday, willing to join in the assistance. The union immediately convened a temporary meeting, chaired by Xu A'mei, to report to the representatives on the course of the forced strike and welcome their participation. Immediately, methods for all future actions were discussed.

Yesterday's General Meeting: After the tragedy, the union held a general meeting in the afternoon, with a total of more than seven hundred workers attending. The municipal party committee specially sent comrades Zhang Yaoming and Gao Xizhong to attend and provide guidance. The various union support associations also sent Lu Jingshi and Zhao Zhenhui as representatives to attend. Chen Puzhu served as chairman and Ai attended. After the ceremony, the chairman reported on the course of the tragedy and said that our workers' actions in going to the club today were extremely civilized. Unexpectedly, the running dogs had already fled without a trace. The French police actually believed that our workers were disrupting public order, without asking the circumstances, and opened fire and strafed, killing one of our Chinese people and shooting dozens of workers. From this point of view, the imperialists are actually treating us with the means of slaughtering dogs. If this is tolerable, what is not tolerable? We hope that all workers will work together. Then various motions were discussed: (1) Prepare a document stating the course of the tragedy and submit it to the higher-level agencies for unified negotiations. (2) Ask the support associations to expand publicity. (3) Petition to organize a support association for the tragedy. (4) Stipulate future work guidelines. It did not disperse until about 6:00 PM.

Tram Service Suspended: There were only twelve trams running the day before. Yesterday, after the tragedy, all twelve trams were also uniformly suspended. Many Chinese and Vietnamese police officers are stationed in the company, waiting with guns, in a serious state. At 1:15 PM, the company suddenly intended to resume service, for a total of three trams, but it soon stopped. Then, a few more trams were dispatched.

Warning to the French Consul: Although this strike is due to the oppression of capitalists, the authorities of the French Concession cannot shirk their responsibility either. The French consul has not intervened in this matter and intends to send a letter of warning today, stating the act of being forced to strike, hoping to uphold justice and properly mediate in order to strengthen Sino-French relations.

Martial Law Yesterday: The French Concession has been under extremely strict guard for days. After yesterday's tragedy, it felt even more tense. The atmosphere was serious on each road and at each stronghold. At 6:00 PM, the iron gates at the borders of the Chinese Concession were closed.

Cable to Protest: Because of the tragedy of the French-owned water and electricity labor strike, the Huadong News reporter went to the municipal party committee at around 12:00 PM yesterday to consult Chen Junyi, a standing committee member of the civil training association. His statement was roughly as follows: I have not yet received a detailed report on the details of this case, but I heard that one person died and three people were injured. The municipal party committee will stop office hours this afternoon (ie, yesterday) and will not be able to convene a meeting to decide on countermeasures, but it has already sent a telegram to the central government to ask for instructions and ordered the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to promptly protest to the French authorities. Moreover, the industrial and commercial circles in Shanghai have also heard that they are preparing countermeasures. The error in this tragedy lies entirely with the factory side. The factory workers' wages average only about twenty yuan per person. Now the price of rice is outside of twenty yuan. How can a family of eight make ends meet? Moreover, the factory's business is growing and developing. Recently, it has increased the salaries of French employees, even to the extent that each person can be increased by an average of over two hundred taels, but it absolutely does not increase the salaries of the workers who are living a hard life. Even after the workers resolved to go on strike, before the Bureau of Social Affairs mediated, the factory ridiculed the workers for not having the courage to strike, forcing a strike. Everyone knows this. Workers struggling for food and clothing is a common thing. In addition, I am also quite strange about the French Consul General. It seems that the French Consul General wants to resolve the expansion of the labor strike. We must know that if we want to resolve everything, we must cure the root cause. The way to cure the root cause now is to make the water and electricity company sincerely accept the mediation of the government. There is no other way. But now the police are arresting people and shooting them. At first, it was a stopgap measure, that is, abandoning the root and pursuing the branches. Therefore, the strike is getting bigger and bigger. Today, it has changed from a small labor-capital dispute to a labor strike. Today, it has changed from a factory's labor strike to a tragedy in the French Concession, that is, it has become an international negotiation. It is also within expectations that reactionary elements have decided to engage in and mix in to disrupt the event, that is, to create an incident similar to the May 30th Massacre. The French Consul General does not cure the root cause but specializes in the stopgap measure, then this responsibility is naturally borne by the French Consul General in the future, and it is also an extremely foolish thing.

This is a very legitimate and reasonable thing. Unexpectedly, the evil French imperialist capitalists are accustomed to implementing imperialist oppressive and destructive methods and have severely rejected your demands, resulting in an unavoidable strike. What working people rely on is nothing more than a small amount of wages, and there is no other source to help workers' lives. Yesterday, a group of running dogs convened a meeting in the club to disrupt the strike discipline. All the workers felt that the running dogs dared to illegally destroy it. Where should the strike discipline be placed? How can the lives of the whole body be sacrificed for the sake of their few running dogs? Therefore, the inspection team was supervised and entered the club to prohibit the meeting. At that time, the running dogs had already heard the news and scattered and avoided. The entire inspection team led the team out, just to reach the intersection. Unexpectedly, the capitalists had colluded with the police in advance and ordered a large number of armed police officers. When they saw the crowd, they fired their guns without asking the reason, and stray bullets were like rain. At that time, a certain citizen (the name is not listed because it has not been verified) who was passing by also succumbed to stray bullets and died. Two workers were seriously injured and twenty-three were arrested. Fellow citizens, we know that the establishment of police stations in the concessions was originally intended to protect residents and maintain public order. Even if the inspection team had improper actions at the time, it could have been arrested and prosecuted in accordance with the law. How could it be possible to fire a gun indiscriminately and launch a random strafing? What did the citizens do to deserve this toxic creation? If we do not submit a serious negotiation and punish the murderer in accordance with the law, in the future, every citizen of the concession can be killed by it. The association believes that this tragic murder case has actually created a second May 30th, which is of international importance. We hope that all fellow citizens will wake up early and make practical assistance to win glory for the country and avenge our compatriots. The time is urgent and cannot be delayed. This ant has achieved the final victory with the collective nature of the mantis struggle. Not only are the French businessmen and workers grateful and weeping, but also the future of the nation is fortunate. The association is willing to lead the power of 800,000 workers in the city to be its backing. If imperialism is not overthrown for one day, the spirit of struggle will not stop for one day. The book is urgent and inexhaustible. I would like to tell you that

The Fifth District and Seventh Branch of this city aided the French-owned water and electricity striking workers' document, Shanghai trade unions aided French-owned water and electricity union support association comrades publicly aware, the French-owned water and electricity capitalists, relying on the power of imperialist tyranny, have oppressed workers in every way, and thousands of people are living in an upside-down position every day. The reasons are not inconsistent, but the French capitalists not only do not accept the workers' requests, but also block the factory gate and refuse to allow workers to enter the factory, forcing a strike. In an instant, a month has passed. The capitalist attitude is firm, and the strike is expanding day by day. May Statistical Report on Household Registration in This City 125

The Municipal Police Bureau has previously reported to this newspaper on the changes in household registration within the city for the month of April. Now, we have received the Bureau's report for May. The total number of households in each district of the city is 185,684 principal households and 164,739 attached households. The population consists of 949,718 males and 701,907 females. The number of foreign households is 2,005, with a population of 9,465. The total number of households counted is 352,428, with a total population of 1,661,090. Within the Special District, the total population of the International Settlement remains as previously reported, with 810,279 Chinese and 29,947 foreigners. The total population of the French Concession, based on a survey conducted in April of this year, is 421,885 Chinese and 12,922 foreigners. Adding these totals, the city's population is 2,936,123, an increase of 8,265 from April.

Social Affairs Bureau Admonishes Rice Industry 126

Listing Points to Note and Ordering Compliance

Following the resumption of independent buying and selling by rice merchants at rice markets, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, fearing that rice merchants might once again engage in under-the-table price adjustments, harming the people's food supply, has specifically listed points to note, ordering all rice industry associations to comply and to make them known to the public. The points to note are recorded below: (1) Investigations have revealed that the past occurrences of price adjustments were due to the inability to strictly differentiate prices between high-quality and lower-quality rice, leading to the undermining of price limits. Since this order, the maximum price for top-quality white rice is limited to 21 yuan. High-quality and lower-quality rice must be strictly priced according to their grade. It is forbidden to sell lower-quality rice at the price of high-quality rice when high-quality rice is out of stock. Violators will be punished as if they were engaging in price adjustments. (2) Furthermore, investigations have revealed that when the price of Japonica rice rises, some mix higher and lower grades together for pricing, or bundle it with a certain percentage of Indica rice, which is effectively the same as price adjustment. In the future, if any of the above situations occur, they will be treated as price adjustment offenses. (3) Unscrupulous rice merchants often mix Indica rice into Japonica rice, hoping to gain illicit profits, which is extremely deceitful. Rice shops and vendors should be held responsible for sampling and inspecting at any time. Once discovered, they should immediately report to this Bureau for punishment. Those who collude to conceal the matter will be punished together. (4) After price evaluation, rice should be immediately unloaded. If merchants dare to refuse to sell, rice shops should be held responsible for immediately reporting to the Bureau, which will sell the rice on their behalf, and a fine of one yuan per picul will be imposed, which will be used as funding for affordable rice. (5) If, after price evaluation, the quality of the rice is found to have deteriorated, it should be re-evaluated immediately, and no disputes should be allowed. (6) The evaluation of rice will still be handled according to custom. If any underweight measurements are discovered, the rice shop will be responsible for compensation, and the measurer will be sent to the Bureau for punishment. If rice merchants use gratuities, leading to underweight measurements, the original vendor will be responsible for sending the rice merchant to the Bureau for punishment. (7) During the open price evaluation period, all rice shops purchasing rice from rice markets should obtain a rice purchase certificate from the Rice Organization Association and use the certificate to purchase from wholesalers. The wholesalers will separately record the number of piculs purchased and the price per picul, affixing a seal as proof. Purchasing rice without a certificate or inaccurate record-keeping will be punished as if engaging in price adjustments. (8) Rice boats selling rice should be allocated by each wholesaler for sale and should not be directly negotiated for purchase by a small number of shops. Violators will be punished according to the severity of the circumstances, in accordance with price adjustment penalties.

Rice Businesses Must Obtain Rice Purchase Certificates 127

Purchasing Rice Without a Certificate or Inaccurate Record-Keeping Will Be Punished

The Rice Business Association Reorganization Committee hereby announces to all rice businesses:

###

###

###

###

Page 14 128

To Whom It May Concern: On the 21st of this month, we received Instruction No. 2590 from the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, which stated: "In order to ensure compliance, it has been observed that rice arriving from the river is now being independently bought and sold by wholesalers and shops. Given that rice prices have not yet fallen, there are concerns that rice shops may compete to purchase rice, offering price adjustments to rice merchants privately, which would be in violation of the law. To prevent such issues from arising, this Bureau hereby instructs the Association to immediately prepare rice purchase certificates and notify fellow businesses to obtain them. Starting from the 22nd of this month, all rice purchased from the North and South Market rice markets must be registered by the rice market with the certificate, indicating the number of piculs and price, and stamped as proof. Purchasing rice without a certificate or inaccurate record-keeping will be punished according to the price adjustment regulations for rice markets. You are hereby instructed to ensure that all fellow businesses comply. This is imperative!" In compliance with this instruction, we have prepared rice purchase certificates for all businesses to obtain. Hereafter, all rice businesses purchasing rice from wholesalers must first go to the Association's North Market office (old site of Tongxing Firm, west of Xinzha Bridge in the North Market) to affix a seal, sign a pledge, and obtain the certificate. Those businesses obtaining certificates must bring their shop's official seal to affix to the certificate at the Association's North Market office. This matter is officially mandated, so please ensure compliance. Furthermore, businesses within the International Settlement should bring one silver dollar to obtain the license for the second half of the year. This announcement is hereby issued.

Police Bureau Arrests Chou Luanxie 129

Escorted to Garrison Headquarters

The Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau arrested reactionary element Pan Qingzeng in December of last year. According to his confession, Chou Luanxie, commander-in-chief of the Eastern Route Army, had established an organization in Shanghai, appointed false positions, and attempted to incite rebellion. The Bureau dispatched officers to conduct a thorough investigation. On June 18th of this year, Chou Luanxie and an accomplice were arrested near Nanyang Bridge in the Chinese district and taken to the Bureau. It is reported that Chou, after being apprehended, frankly described the recruitment of followers and his reactionary plans without any concealment. The Bureau, considering his advanced age, treated him with courtesy. However, as the case involves reactionary activities and serious circumstances, he has been escorted to the Garrison Headquarters for interrogation.
