Actively Opposing 134

The case of the sale of the Shanghai International Settlement's Sino-Foreign Telephone Company to an international company has been finalized. The signing of the agreement and payment are scheduled for the end of October. The Chinese residents in the Settlement, due to the matter's connection to national sovereignty and close impact on the interests of the residents, have repeatedly expressed their strong opposition. Now, due to the urgency of the situation, various public organizations have been convening emergency meetings to discuss countermeasures. The Chinese Ratepayers' Association has previously publicly elected Chinese Directors Yuan Ludeng and Chinese Committee Members Xu Xinliu, and three others as committee members to do their best to negotiate with the Municipal Council and are striving to reverse the decision. The Special District Residents' Association held a special committee meeting at 2:00 pm yesterday to discuss the telephone issue. Committee members Qian Longzhang, Yu Hualong, Jiang Xinzhao, Yu Zhongxian, Zhang Xianfang, Qiu Jialiang, and eight others attended. The discussion concluded that the case is of great importance and that the mistakes of the previous Electricity Department issue could not be repeated. The Association, representing all residents, is determined to protect national sovereignty and safeguard the public interest of merchants and residents and is determined to oppose the sale to the end, without hesitation. On the one hand, they will contact various public organizations to unite and carry out opposition; on the other hand, they will raise funds to develop proactive countermeasures. The following measures were decided upon: (1) Committee Member Jiang Xinzhao proposed sending a letter to the Chinese Ratepayers' Association to convene a representative assembly of taxpayers throughout the district as soon as possible to urgently discuss the opposition to the telephone sale. The proposal was approved and a letter of recommendation will be sent immediately. (2) Committee Member Qiu Jialiang proposed that there has been a recent initiative to form a Chinese Telephone Users' Association, but its contents, membership, and direction are unknown to the outside world. There are tens of thousands of Chinese telephone users in the Settlement. As a representative organization of the residents, this Association should immediately send representatives to investigate and make contact in order to unite efforts and strengthen the force. The proposal was approved and Committee Members Yu Hualong and Yu Zhongxian were appointed as representatives to make contact immediately. A second committee meeting is scheduled for this afternoon. In addition, the Chamber of Commerce has already expressed its serious concern.

International Radio Station Buildings 135

Ministry of Communications Dispatches Personnel for Inspection

The construction of the International Radio Station buildings of the Ministry of Communications International Communications Radio Station Preparatory Office at 152 Xinzha Road in this city and behind Jinnan University in Zhenru, as well as alongside the East-West County Road of Liuhang in Baoshan County, has been completed after commencing on March 12th, lasting four months. The Ministry of Communications has dispatched technical officers Li Fushen and Shen Pinhou from Beijing to Shanghai for inspection. Director Zhang Chenghu of the Office's Engineering Section is supervising the expedited installation of the station's equipment, which is expected to be completed by the end of October. Formal communication with Europe and the United States is expected to commence within the year.

Reporters from various newspapers, in order to ascertain the latest construction progress of the radio station, visited the International Communications Radio Station Preparatory Office at 152 Xinzha Road in this city to inquire about all the details. According to Zhao Yilin, director of the General Affairs Section, and Zhang Chenghu, director of the Engineering Section, the radio station being constructed in Shanghai includes the Sino-American, Sino-German, Sino-French Radio Stations and the International Communications Branch Station, as well as the Dalei Foreign Firm leased radio station. The locations of the transmitter stations for the Sino-American, Sino-German, and Sino-French Radio Stations are behind Jinnan University in Zhenru, Shanghai, while the location of the receiver station is in Liuhang, Baoshan County. The central control room is located in the Sassoon House at the intersection of Renji Road in this city. The International Communications Branch Station's transmitter station is located next to the Municipal Government in Fenlin Bridge, Shanghai, while the receiver station is in Liuhang, Baoshan County. The central control room is also located in the Sassoon House. The Dalei Foreign Firm leased radio station is attached to the International Branch Station in Fenlin Bridge. It is reported that the projects for the International Branch Station and the Dalei Foreign Firm leased radio station were completed early and have already commenced formal communications. They were transferred to the Shanghai Wireless Radio Management Office last month and the month before, respectively. The progress of the construction of the transmitter station of the Zhenru Radio Station is approximately as follows: (1) The Sino-American and Sino-German transmitter station buildings and staff dormitories have been completed and have been inspected by personnel dispatched by the Ministry of Communications. The foundation for the machinery is now being built. (2) The Sino-French transmitter station building project will be completed soon. (3) The internal roads of the transmitter station are being paved. (4) The Taopu West Road leading to Zhenru Railway Station has been completed, and the bridge over the river is more than half finished. (5) Self-flowing wells have been dug, and the water tower is being built. (6) The transmitter antenna poles for the Sino-American and Sino-German radio stations have been erected. The antenna network is now being hung. (7) One Sino-French transmitter antenna has been completed. (8) The machinery for the Sino-American and Sino-German radio stations has been transported from Shanghai in succession and will be installed immediately. The cold water pipes and wiring ducts inside the station have been installed. (9) The remote control cables leading to Shanghai will be erected and strung soon. (10) The power line poles leading to Shanghai have been erected. The progress of the construction of the receiver station of the Liuhang Radio Station is as follows: (1) The receiver station buildings and staff dormitories have been completed and have been inspected by personnel dispatched by the Ministry of Communications. (2) The internal roads of the receiver station are being paved. (3) The power plant building will be completed soon. Power generation will commence as soon as the machinery is installed. (4) The Sino-American receiver antenna has been completely completed. (5) Two Sino-French receiver antennas have been erected. (6) The installation of the machinery for the Sino-American radio station has commenced and will be completed next month. (7) The machinery for the Sino-French radio station will be transported and installed immediately. (8) The remote control cables leading to Shanghai will be erected and strung soon. Despite the recent hot weather, the staff members are working diligently, and it is expected that all projects will be completed by the end of October. Formal communication will be prepared within the year.

(7) Sales Group: 4:00 pm on the fourth Wednesday of each month. (8) Design Group: 4:00 pm on the fourth Friday of each month. According to Mr. Shi Youming, the association's executive director, specialized committees of each group can start from next month, to successively hold meetings to discuss practical work. Members of the association who wish to join which group will also be solicited by letter.

Overseas Chinese Return to Investigate Industries 137

Establishing a General Office in Shanghai

Raising Huge Sums for an Industrial Bank

Overseas Chinese merchants from various ports, in order to revitalize domestic industry and seek the development of domestic production, have initiated and organized the Overseas Chinese Industrial Return and Investigation Delegation to return to the country and go to the North and South to earnestly investigate various products as a preparation for starting operations. Yesterday, a portion of the delegation arrived in Shanghai and is currently staying at a foreign hotel on Baidu Bridge. The entire delegation consists of 25 people, with five people per team. According to a friend who introduced the reporter from the Guowen News Agency to Mr. Li Hairu of the delegation, the delegation will establish a general office in Shanghai on Hualong Road in the French Concession. All members of the delegation are wealthy overseas Chinese merchants who value practical work and are unwilling to engage in unnecessary extravagance and social events. The time limit for this return and investigation is six months. The plan is to establish a large-scale industrial bank in the country, with capital of more than 20 million. Because gold is expensive and silver is cheap at this time, it is extremely cost-effective for overseas Chinese to invest in their motherland, which is a once-in-a-lifetime opportunity. Once the investigation is clear, a plan will be drawn up to obtain special rights from the government before conducting various industries, and to create opportunities to arouse the national public to work together to produce and recover rights, in order to achieve the purpose of saving the country through production.

Shipping Costs to India Rise Sharply 139

Since the rise in gold and the decline in silver, the monetary systems of various countries in the world have been soaring, while the Chinese silver dollar has been falling. The prices of foreign goods arriving in China have increased almost without exception. Shipping companies in Shanghai have increased freight rates to foreign countries one after another, except for shipments to India. Now, the major Sino-Indian shipping companies, including British India Steam Navigation Company, Nippon Yusen Kaisha, Osaka Shosen Kaisha, and Jardine Matheson, have discussed increasing freight rates for Chinese goods to India. It is reported that it has been agreed to implement the increase from August 1st. The details are as follows:

Freight rates to be increased: Within the Sino-Indian routes, there is a freight rate association in Shanghai. Member shipping companies cannot arbitrarily increase or decrease freight rates. Freight rates on this route have been collected in silver taels. Since the rise in gold, the Indian rupee has risen from 56 taels to 107 taels and 5 qian. Various companies, facing huge losses, have proposed increasing the freight rates for Shanghai export goods to Bombay and Calcutta from August 1st. Generally, the increase is about 20%, but some goods may increase by as much as 40%. For example, the freight rate for one ton of miscellaneous goods to India, originally set at 20 taels, is now increased to 27 taels. Silk, tea, and satin are also subject to increased rates. The shipping rate schedule is currently being revised and is expected to be revised and announced within a day or two.

Sharp decline in silk goods: Silk goods are the largest item of Chinese cargo shipped to India, with xiaofang (small textiles) accounting for the largest share of exports. Gao Pei and Samsung Foreign Firms in Shanghai specialize in procuring and transporting this commodity to Bombay and other ports. During the peak season, silk goods worth approximately 3 million yuan were shipped each month. Since the Gandhi movement in India, purchasers of Chinese goods in various parts of India have stopped purchasing and transporting them, and the export route for xiaofang has been blocked. Recently, there has been a sharp decline in the number of Chinese silk goods shipped to Bombay from Shanghai.

Record of the Shanghai County Government Meeting 140

The Shanghai County Government held its 43rd County Government Meeting yesterday. More than ten bureau chiefs from the county attended. The meeting commenced at 2:00 pm, presided over by County Magistrate Yan and recorded by Hu Gongshou. Important resolutions were made: (1) Regarding the use of educational public property by the Xinpu Yutang without a contract, it was resolved that the Education Bureau should contact the Xinpu Yutang charitable organization to complete the procedures. (2) Regarding the discussion of the methods for People's Schools, it was resolved to implement the methods for People's Schools drafted by the Education Bureau and to stipulate an operating expense of 180 yuan. The Education Bureau was designated to be responsible for organizing and proceeding immediately. (3) Regarding the handling of the Yu Tang expenses and the collection of land tax, it was resolved that for land tax collection exceeding the prescribed limit, the local people should formulate other methods, prepare a detailed budget, and submit it to the county for forwarding for filing. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 pm.

Central Bank Inspection Report 145

The sixtieth inspection report of the Central Bank's issuance reserves states: According to Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, this committee is responsible for inspecting the reserve fund for the issuance of convertible banknotes by this bank. We hereby announce the results of the sixtieth inspection conducted on July 19th, 19th year of the Republic of China, at the Issuing Bureau of this bank, as follows: The total amount of convertible banknotes issued is 17,092,748 silver dollars, including 16,014,491 silver dollar banknotes and 1,078,257 silver dollars in subsidiary currency banknotes. The total amount of convertible banknote reserves is 17,092,748 silver dollars, including 14,263,249.60 silver dollars in cash reserves. This cash reserve is held in the bank's issuing treasury at 11,291,372.73 silver dollars, held in branches in various ports at 1,179,235.14 silver dollars, and deposited with other banks at 1,792,641.73 silver dollars. The guarantee reserve, converted to silver dollars, is 2,829,498.40 silver dollars. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank Convertible Banknote Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is less than 40%, which is in compliance with the regulations. This report is hereby made. July 20th, 19th year of the Republic of China. Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Li Fusun; Supervisors, Wang Jingli, Ju Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Ji.

Tragedy Outside Songkou 147

Retrieving Wooden Boxes Led to a Sudden Explosion

Shipowner and Son Blown Up on the Spot

Two Shipmates Slightly Injured

At around 2:00 p.m. the day before yesterday, a loud noise was suddenly heard on the sea off Bailonggang outside Wusongkou. After investigation, it was learned that a large number of wooden boxes were floating on the sea surface at that location. Several sand dredging boats happened to pass by and saw them, so they rushed to retrieve the wooden boxes. Suddenly, an explosion occurred, resulting in a tragedy. Two boatmen were blown up on the spot and two others were injured. The details are as follows:

Wooden Boxes Discovered on the Sea Surface At around 2:00 p.m. yesterday, a large number of wooden boxes, hundreds of them, resembling soap boxes, were suddenly discovered on the sea surface about seventy miles outside Wusongkou, floating and drifting with the waves.

Boatmen Rushed to Retrieve Them Several Ningbo fishing boats, loaded with sand dredged from Dinghai, Zhejiang, and en route to Shanghai for sale, passed by the area. Seeing countless wooden boxes floating on the sea, the boatmen rushed to retrieve them. Just as they were rejoicing, the tragedy occurred as a result.

Wooden Boxes Exploded Suddenly The boxes retrieved by the boatmen were all empty inside. The Jin Taimao sand dredging boat retrieved more than thirty wooden boxes, one of which was tightly sealed. Unexpectedly, while they were trying to open it, the box was slightly shaken and suddenly exploded. With a loud bang, the shipowner Ni A'ang and his son A'bang were instantly killed, and shipmates He Asheng and Zhi Abing were injured.

Shipowner's Flesh and Blood Flew Everywhere Shipowner Ni A'ang was from Dinghai, 54 years old, and his son A'bang was 22 years old. When the box exploded, the father and son's flesh and blood flew everywhere, their intestines spilled out, and their limbs were broken. Blood splattered throughout the cabin, a horrific sight. At that time, shipmates He Bingsheng and Zhi Ajiong were fortunately in the stern cabin and only suffered minor injuries to their faces and other areas. After the accident, the shipmates, unable to do anything because the boat was at sea, left one person to watch the boat and another came to Song to inform a fellow villager, Mr. So-and-so, to report to Shanghai. The Ni shipowner's nephew arrived in Song yesterday morning, bought coffins and clothing, and hired a boat to go to collect the bodies for burial in their hometown.

Dye Merchant Xie Keming Kidnapped 148

Kidnapped on His Way Home for Lunch

A Car Was Parked on the Roadside in Advance

At around 12:30 p.m. yesterday, a kidnapping case occurred near Jiangxi Road and Sijing Road. The kidnapped person was Xie Keming, a native of Ningbo, who served as the director of the dye department at De Fu Foreign Firm at 68 Sichuan Road. His family lived at Renjihao, 630 Dongqipan Street. In addition to working at De Fu Foreign Firm, Xie also ran his own dye business. At around 12:15 p.m. yesterday, Xie Keming took his private chartered car from 68 Sichuan Road to the warehouse, preparing to return to Renjihao on Dongqipan Street for lunch. Unexpectedly, when the car reached the intersection of Jiangxi Road and Sijing Road, they saw a car parked on the east side of the road. As Xie's car was about to return to the car, suddenly three men came forward. One of them held a pistol, forcing the carter to stop moving forward. The two bandits went straight to the car seat and dragged Xie down. Because of the excessive force, the car cushion was also pulled down. After Xie was forced out of the car, he was immediately taken into the car by the bandits and sped west along Sijing Road. In a hurry, the carter was unable to do anything and only saw that the kidnappers' car number was 1750. After receiving the news, the Central Police immediately sent detectives to investigate, but there were no clues for a while. However, it was found that the kidnappers' license plate code was actually forged. Xie had worked at De Fu Foreign Firm for many years, and his family also lived in Shanghai. Xie's carter, Wang A'er, said that the bandit with the gun was wearing a suit, and the car was a black convertible.

The third newly discovered hurricane in the Pacific Ocean has not changed its direction of travel. The Municipal Public Security Bureau Orders Reporting of Handling of Kidnapping Cases 151

The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau issued an order yesterday, stating: "It is found that the table of kidnapping cases submitted by the First Section from various districts has been reviewed. From February 27th to May 6th, there are more than 30 unsolved cases. The table has been copied and circulated to the respective districts and teams, ordering them to check the listed industries under their jurisdiction and urging their subordinates to intensify their efforts to arrest the perpetrators. The respective district chiefs are also responsible for all cases in their respective districts and should urge the police detectives to investigate and arrest the perpetrators, offering rewards based on the severity of the case. The subordinate police officers should also be investigated for their arrest achievements, and their performance should be evaluated and reported accordingly. However, more than a month has passed, and only a few cases have been solved in the various districts, while more than 20 new cases have occurred in the past month. The district chiefs have not yet submitted the reports as ordered, which is a disregard for official orders. The previous order is hereby reiterated, and the respective districts and teams are ordered to immediately urge their subordinates to intensify their efforts to arrest the perpetrators of the new and old cases under their jurisdiction, and to capture the stolen goods and real criminals as many as possible. At the same time, a detailed list of the new and old cases should be submitted, outlining the investigation process, and reported to the respective district chiefs. The respective district chiefs should also comply with the previous order, urging the police detectives to cooperate and strictly investigate, and submit a consolidated report within 15 days from the date of receipt of this document, in accordance with the previous order, for review and reward or punishment. The respective district chiefs must not treat this document as a formality and continue to be negligent, which may cause inconvenience. This order is imperative."

Chen Yuxi's Concubine Comes to Shanghai to Sue for Inheritance 157

Accuses Eldest Son Chen Zhongshan

Husband Died Without Providing Support

Submits Three Requests

The Court Hopes for Reconciliation

Chen Yuxi, a native of Zhenhai, had a large commercial business in Shanghai during his lifetime, including the Bao Chengyuji and Lao Fengxiang silver shops on Nanjing Road, as well as the Housheng, Juyuan, Yisheng, and Sanbei freight forwarding companies, and the Dongyang Nanhua Zhuang. Chen had shares in all of these businesses. After Chen's death, the above-mentioned businesses and other properties he left behind were worth no less than 200,000 yuan, all of which were controlled by his eldest son, Chen Zhongshan. During Yuxi's lifetime, he had not only one wife. There is also a Du family member, who also gave birth to two sons and one daughter, who have been living in the countryside of his hometown. The Du family member is now forty-four years old, and her children are gradually growing up. They need funds for schooling and marriage. Because the eldest son Zhongshan does not provide support, she brought her children from her hometown to Shanghai and hired lawyer Zhan Jifeng to sue Zhongshan in the Special District Court, requesting a division of the inheritance. Her complaint states: "It has been ten years since my late husband Yuxi passed away. During this time, I have supported the family and raised the children, all by myself. I have truly endured hardship. Although my late husband established a will during his lifetime, it was based on the defendant's own opinion, because at that time my late husband was already in his twilight years and did not want to worry about anything. The defendant took control of all the properties, which were worth about 200,000 yuan. The defendant took this opportunity to establish a will. I am a woman and do not know how to read. I have never seen the will and do not know its contents. The defendant has also not made the will public, so it is difficult to list all the properties. However, as far as I know, the Bao Chengyuji and Lao Fengxiang silver shops, the Housheng, Juyuan, Yisheng, and Sanbei freight forwarding companies, and the Dongyang Nanhua store all have shares that have been swallowed up. There are also many more that I do not know about. After my late husband's death, the defendant did not bring me to live in Shanghai, but left me in a poor and remote village. He did not care about his half-siblings. They are now in urgent need of funds for schooling and marriage. I have repeatedly reasoned with him, but the defendant has turned a deaf ear. This is unbearable. Therefore, I request that the defendant be summoned to court and ordered to (1) hand over the will, (2) disclose the detailed accounts of the shares of the various shops left behind, and (3) fairly divide the inheritance." Based on the complaint, the court issued a warrant ordering officials to summon the defendant to appear in court at 241 Baoyufang, South Chengdu Road, for trial. Yesterday morning, Judge Yang Yi opened the court. The defendant Chen Zhongshan did not appear. According to his representative lawyer, the defendant suffers from mental illness and therefore could not appear. The plaintiff's lawyer Zhan Jifeng also stated that the subject matter of the lawsuit has not yet been determined. Once the amount of property is clear, the litigation fees will be paid in accordance with the regulations. Judge Yang believed that this kind of family dispute is best resolved through reconciliation, and advised both lawyers to go out and mediate. Lawyer Zhan said that he would abide by the court's goodwill and requested that the case be postponed. If reconciliation fails, he would request that the defendant be summoned to court, because there are many factual issues in dispute. The defendant's lawyer also presented three copies of the will to the court. Judge Yang then ordered the hearing to be rescheduled and allowed the plaintiff to copy the will for study.

Shen Xinyi and Two Others Acquitted 158

The Kidnapping of Xi Xiangquan, a Resident of Er Tu Township, Nanhui County, Caused a Sensation

Xi Xiangquan, a resident of Er Tu Township, Nanhui County, was kidnapped, involving his brother Xi Xianglin and others. The local court has investigated and made a judgment. Xi Xiangquan was kidnapped in September of the 17th year of the Republic of China and redeemed at the end of October. At the end of that year, Cao Yongqi, the director of the Nanhui County Public Security Bureau, colluded with a local tycoon named Yang, intending to extort a huge sum of money from Xi's brother, Xi Xianglin. First, he made someone suggest it, and then, on New Year's Eve, he arrested Xi Xianglin. On the way, he met Shen Xinyi and Tan Xinglou, who were also arrested for violating the night curfew. Xi Xianglin offered to pay a ransom, but Xi refused. After being taken to the bureau, they were initially treated well in the receiving and dispatch office and persuaded to pay a bribe. Later, they were forced to confess to being communists by using torture. Xi and the other two refused to confess. Then, they were frightened into reporting the kidnapping of Xi Xiangquan. At that time, County Magistrate Shen Yuzhong was on leave in Shanghai, and Cao Yongqi colluded with Section Chief Liu of the county government. They were suddenly transferred to the county detention center and then brought back to the Public Security Bureau, where they were tortured to force a confession. After half a month, they were sent to the county government. Shen Xinyi and others repeatedly appealed to the Judicial Yuan, the Ministry of Justice, the provincial government, and the High Court, accusing the county magistrate of dereliction of duty and Cao Yongqi of abuse of torture and violation of the law. The High Court approved the transfer of the case to the Shanghai Local Court for trial. Prosecutor Zhu Jun first investigated and found it suspicious, and filed a public prosecution. Judge Qian Chengjun then investigated and interrogated Xi Xianglin, who was defended by lawyer Wei Wangzeng. Shen Xinyi also hired lawyer Wang Youlin to defend him, and Tan Xinglou was also assigned lawyer Wang Zengxian by Judge Qian. The debate was held in court a few days ago, and Prosecutor Wang Sixian attended and stated that although the case had been prosecuted, after careful examination of the entire file, the three defendants in this case were actually wronged, and the plaintiff's claims were unreliable. Yesterday morning, the judgment was announced: Shen Xinyi, Tan Xinglou, and Xi Xianglin were all acquitted. Judge Qian then warned the three defendants to be safe and abide by the law outside and not to cause trouble. Thus, the scandalous kidnapping case that caused a sensation came to an end. It is heard that the real kidnappers, Wang Yinglong and two others, have been executed by firing squad in Nanhui County for other cases.

The Zhen Fengtai Lawsuit Was Opened Again Yesterday 159

New Store Uses Old Account Books

Zhu Mu, a native of Hubei, and Zhang Binghui, the manager of the Yu Fengtai Hotel, and Hu Baohua, Zhou Maolin, and others opened the Zhen Fengtai Shaoxing Hotel on North Sichuan Road. The court then appointed accountant Zhao Zuwei to appraise the account books, and the report stated that there were indeed flaws in the account books. Zhu Mu then filed a complaint with the Procuratorate, accusing Zhang Binghui, Hu Baohua, Zhou Maolin, Hu Guoan, and others of forging documents and instigating Wang Jingqing to publicly insult him with filthy objects. The prosecutor then released the defendants on bail and filed a public prosecution, which is the fourth lawsuit. The lawsuits have been going on for ten months. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhao of the Criminal Court opened the trial. Zhu Mu testified, "I and them opened the store together. At that time, the capital was 2,000 yuan. I invested 500 yuan. Hu Baohua was appointed as the manager, Zhang Binghui as the supervisor, Zhou Maolin as the assistant, and I was responsible for checking the accounts. After opening in December of the 17th year of the Republic of China, I repeatedly asked them to check the accounts, but they refused to allow me to see them, so I was suspicious. In March of the 18th year, I requested to withdraw my shares. They said that I had to wait until the Dragon Boat Festival, and then said that I had to wait for half a year to settle the accounts. Unexpectedly, by the Mid-Autumn Festival, they did not return the money to me. On the contrary, they said that the 2,000 yuan of capital had been almost completely lost and that I still had to find money. But Hu Baohua is the manager, but he is not in the store. He only entrusted his father to act as his agent. His father is a Taoist priest. How can he manage the store affairs and not allow me to check the accounts? After the lawsuit, the first instance judge did not understand, so I appealed. Judge Zhao opened the court and ordered me to take the account books for the appointed accountant to appraise. There were indeed acts of forgery, so I ordered the criminal case to be resolved first. But they swallowed my shares and stuffed feces in me. I really suffered too much. I ask for an investigation." Zhang Binghui testified, "I live at 1793 Hongkou. Zhu Mu was checking the accounts in the store every day. The accounts were managed by the manager. The appraisal by accountant Zhao Zuwei was a correct procedure. There are some flaws. We are all illiterate and cannot do the accounts. The capital of 2,000 yuan was used up due to large expenses, and there was a shortage of more than 600 yuan." The official asked, "Why are the account books fake?" He replied, "Because of economic reasons, we bought old account books and account books that had been used in old stores." The official said, "How can a new store not even be able to afford account books? This is a joke." At this point, he asked Hu Baohua, who testified that he was the manager. He asked, "Why are the account books fake?" He replied, "Because the capital is small, we used old books, so there is the appearance of being unbound and scribbled." The official asked, "How can a person who does business not know the rules? An account book only costs a few cents. How can a store owner not afford it?" He ordered him to step down and then asked Zhou Maolin, who testified the same as before. At this point, the accountants Zhang Xingsheng and Hu Guoan also testified that because the capital in the store was small, for economic reasons, they either used old account books from elsewhere or bought old account books from old goods stalls and unbound them for use. The official believed that the facts of the case were clear, but the account books had not yet been transferred from the civil court, so he ordered that the debate be rescheduled for the 28th of this month, and then ordered them to leave the court.

Five Suspects Arrested in Tin Theft Case 160

Judgment on the Case of Russian Man in Car Injuring Hu Yu-fang 161

Hu Yu-fang, a student at St. John's University, was riding a motorized bicycle on Yu Yuan Road in western Shanghai in March of this year when a car from Lai Yi Auto Company sped towards him and collided with Hu's bicycle, resulting in damage to the vehicle and injuries to Hu. Hu was treated at a hospital and the damaged bicycle was repaired, incurring losses. The Special District Court held several hearings, summoned witnesses, and conducted thorough investigations. The police station summoned the accused Englishman for questioning. It was determined that there were no family members to claim the body, so it was ordered to be photographed and collected by the church. Min Long-yin Commits Suicide Due to Economic Hardship 166

Min Long-yin, a 34-year-old man from Huzhou, used to be in the mat business, but is now unemployed. On the 18th, he checked into a room at the Nanyang Hotel at No. 15 Rue des Soeurs in the French Concession. Due to the pressure of economic hardship, he suddenly had a desperate idea. On the evening of the 19th, he ingested an anesthetic solution to commit suicide. When the poison took effect, the tea room attendant, Song Fa-lin, found out, entered the room, and saw Min foaming at the mouth and unable to speak. He immediately reported to the Xiaodongmen Police Station, who sent Min to Renji Hospital. Because the poison had already taken effect deeply, the rescue was ineffective and he died. The hospital notified the police station, who ordered investigators to transport the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Hall coroner's office. They informed Min Jing-ru, the deceased's uncle (who works at the Tongchang Store in Dadongmen), to come. Yesterday, the Criminal Division of the French Police Station reported to Judge Zhu Cheng of the French Concession Court, who examined the body and confirmed that the deceased had died from poisoning. He ordered the uncle to prepare a coffin and collect the body for burial. After the examination, the body was hastily placed in a coffin and taken to the Huzhou Guild Hall Bing House for temporary storage.

Miss Qiu Bitterly Recounts Encountering a Violent Obstacle Midway 168

The Two Men Should Be Thoroughly Investigated

Around 1:00 AM yesterday morning, a young woman was seen pacing back and forth on the Puxi side of the Santai Wharf in the Nanshi district, and then she jumped into the river. As the tide was rising, the woman immediately sank to the bottom of the river after jumping. The boatmen nearby heard the sound, looked around, and quickly used bamboo poles to rescue her. However, because she had swallowed too much water, her abdomen was swollen and her breathing was faint. They performed surgery to drain the water from her stomach and then gave her ginger soup. The woman gradually woke up and regained her senses. Zhang Guang-han, the guard on duty at the 17th post, was called to the scene and took her back to the first section of the first district. The section chief questioned her and she gave her name as Qiu Mei-mei, 21 years old, from Pudong. She said she lived at No. 11, south of the Xiaohuo train station in Yangsi Bridge, Pudong. Her parents had both died early. She usually relied on her older brother, Qiu Gen-sheng, for support. Because her younger sister, Xiao-mei, who is only nine years old, had recently contracted scabies, she took a ferry to Puxi on the 12th of this month to buy medicine for sores from the Taishan Hall medicinal materials store in the city of Dadongmen. Then, she went to visit relatives at Dananmen. She left around 6:00 PM and then went to Dongjiadu Wharf to

Page 16

board a ferry. After arriving in Pudong, it was already late and the Xiaohuo train had stopped running, so she had no way to return home. She planned to walk, but unexpectedly, on the way, she suddenly encountered two men she did not know who blocked her path and flirted with her. She ignored them, but they forcibly took her to Puxi. She knew that they were not good people and quickly tried to call for help, but was afraid of being harmed, so she reluctantly let them take her. Later, she was lodged at a hotel outside the old North Gate. After one night, she was still watched and was not allowed to move. For nine days, she had been thinking about escaping, but could not find a good opportunity. Around 10:00 PM last night (the day before yesterday), one of the men left to raise money because they had run out. The other man was fast asleep in bed, and she had a chance to escape. She immediately sneaked out of the hotel and hired a car to Dongjiadu in the Nanshi district. When she was about to board a boat to cross the river, she suddenly remembered that it had been many days since she left home. She had been indecently insulted by them for no reason. How could she face her family? Furthermore, her family must be very panicked because she had not returned home for many days. If she returned home late at night, it would inevitably cause suspicion. Who would speak out for the injustice she suffered? At this point, she was in a dilemma. While she was pondering silently, the tide was rising and she suddenly felt clear-headed. After a long time of silence, she felt that there was no fun in this troubled world. It would be better to commit suicide by jumping into the river to wash away the accumulated resentment. So she went to the banks of the Santai Wharf and, taking advantage of people not paying attention, jumped in to end her life. Unexpectedly, she was rescued by the boatmen and taken into custody by the police. After speaking, she cried bitterly, which made the viewers sad. The section chief considered the case to be a suicide attempt and prepared a document to be sent to the Third Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Wife Who Worked as a Streetcar Ticket Inspector 169

Escaped Twice and Never Returned

Ticket inspector Requests Divorce

Liu Tian-cheng, a native of Yancheng who works as a ticket inspector for the streetcar company in the International Settlement, lives at No. 145 Xiangyan Bridge, Hongkou. Ten years ago, he married Xu Qi-bao, a 20-year-old woman, through a matchmaker (Xu is now 30 years old). However, Xu's nature was promiscuous and she did not abide by the virtues of a wife. She ran away several times. In August of the 17th year of the Republic, Xu ran away from her husband. Liu Tian-cheng found out where she was hiding and reported her to the police, who arrested the adulterer and adulteress and transferred them to the local court. Liu did not want to pursue the matter further, so the man and woman were released on bail. In April of last year, Xu lured and abducted a Wang-surname child, and was arrested. After investigation and trial, the court sentenced her to six months in prison. She was released in October. On the afternoon of April 27th of this year, Xu took the opportunity to run away again. Liu Tian-cheng could not bear the burden and filed a divorce lawsuit with the local court, stating that the defendant, Liu Xu (i.e., Xu Qi-bao) had committed all kinds of evil deeds and violated criminal laws, such as adultery and abduction, all of which were documented in the court. This time, she relapsed and ran away again, taking with her 37 yuan in silver, two gold rings, one pair of gold bracelets, and dozens of pieces of clothing, disappearing without a trace. He reported this to the Fourth District First Section Police Station for record. Because she is now hiding and not showing her face, he fears that she is with bandits and that accidents may occur. Moreover, with the defendant's behavior, it is difficult to live together until old age, so he has to divorce her to avoid future troubles. Yesterday morning, Judge Du held a hearing. Because the defendant's address was unknown, she could not be served and did not appear in court. Only the plaintiff, Liu Tian-cheng, appeared and stated that he was 46 years old and currently worked as a streetcar ticket inspector in the British Concession, and stated the previous situation, requesting a divorce judgment. The judge, after receiving the testimony, ordered him to leave and await consideration.

Old Woman Uses Sweet Words to Lure Young Girl 171

Nearly Sold, Fortunately No Patron

The girl, Yang A-mei, is only fifteen years old and originally from Shanghai. Because her parents died in Shanghai when she was five years old, she went to Suzhou to live with her maternal grandmother. Ten years passed. On the 21st of last month, a woman named Ni You-shi from Haimen saw the girl in Suzhou and used sweet words to lure her, saying that if she came to Shanghai with her, she would send her to school, hire a nanny to serve her, and that she had a lot of gold jewelry that she would give to her in the future. A-mei was indeed deceived by the woman and escaped to Shanghai with her. The woman originally wanted to sell the girl, but she has been lingering until now and still has no patron. At 2:00 PM the day before yesterday, the woman took the girl out again. While walking on Kunming Road, detective Yang Xi-chen saw them and felt that their appearance was suspicious, so he questioned them. The woman felt guilty and answered evasively. The girl repented and told the truth. Yang brought them both to the Huishan Police Station. Yesterday morning, Feng, a judge, summoned them to the Special District Court. A-mei described in detail how she had been abducted, saying that after arriving in Shanghai, she had no fixed residence and was not allowed to go out alone every day. Now she desperately wanted to return to Suzhou. When questioned, Ni You-shi said that she was originally acquainted with the girl's maternal grandmother, and that she had informed her of her bringing the girl to Shanghai, and that it was not abduction for the purpose of selling her. The court ordered the girl to be temporarily detained at the Jiliang Institute, and the defendant to be held for a rescheduled hearing to clarify the facts.

Then, Ma Zhi-gang expressed his opinion, saying that there are no less than 100 wood companies in the south and north. They have been contacted and established associations again and again, but they have been suspended halfway and have not been able to establish a sound organization. Now that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce has issued the Hope Order, we should reorganize according to law and merge with various paint industries to form a legal association. In the future, the rights and happiness of our industry will be unlimited. However, someone must be responsible for the procedures for joint assembly in progress so that it can be established as scheduled. The organization committee should be elected to take special responsibility. Zhang Fu-kang, Ling You-qiao, Zhou Shan-qing, Zhao Hong-zhen, Huang Shou-chun, Zhang Zhong-fu, Ma Zhi-gang, Cai Lan-zhou, Cai You-qing, Zhao Yun-shan, Shen Qi-wen, Ma Ji-liang, Wu Zhong-shan, Wang Yong-lian, Wu Ren-yao, Zhu Ju-ping, Zhang Ming-qia, and Xu Guo-qing were elected as the reorganization committee of the wood industry to share the guidance and joint affairs in the north and south. The crowd unanimously agreed. Then, Lin Zhi-zhou, a guest, gave a lecture on the joint organization methods of industrial and commercial groups and the various inherent rights that should be enjoyed after the establishment. His earnest and detailed analogy was appropriate. Hearing this, the audience was moved. At this point, the bell rang six times, and the meeting was adjourned.

Resolved: Fast and slow long-distance trains are allowed to carry 20 dozens of soda water, and short-distance shuttle trains are allowed to carry half that amount. Send a prompt letter to the catering section for verification. (3) Members Zhu A Zhao, Monk, etc., of the Huhang Railway submitted a request to the union, asking to transfer the soda water sales rights to those selling pastries, so as to be the same as the Jinghu Railway. Resolved: To convene all car group leaders, along with those selling tea and pastries on third-class cars, at the union at 9:00 AM on the 15th of this month to discuss solutions. (4) The case of member Zou of the Xining train. Resolved: He has violated Article 29, Section 3 of Chapter 11 of the union's constitution and should be subject to the punishment of revoking his membership and dismissal from work. (5) Member Wang Yunsheng of the Huhang Railway reported to the union on the 8th of this month that substitute Zhou Mingfu was detained by the Garrison Headquarters on suspicion of carrying contraband. Resolved: To send Inspector Zhou Panlin to thoroughly investigate and report back for verification. (C) Temporary motions: (1) Xu Renyi proposed that because the night train tea servers Lu Tingfu, Fang Yonglin, and Guo Huiqing, who have been dismissed from work, have not cleared their financial procedures, a letter should be sent to the Railway Bureau requesting an extension of ten days for the temporary substitute licenses they signed. Resolved: To comply. (2) A letter was sent to the Railway Bureau requesting an additional 15 substitute licenses for the Jinghu Railway, but no reply has been received. How to supplement the current substitutes. Resolved: To consult the catering section on the issue of increasing the number of licenses, and temporarily supplement 25 substitute licenses. Replacements must be selected from those who have not been introduced to the position. (3) Chen Arong introduced Zhou Xiaodi to join the union. Resolved: Approved.

Weather Report 186

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the coastal area will have sunny and hot weather, there will be thunderstorms in the Yangtze River basin, the East China Sea will have southeasterly winds, the Yellow Sea will have winds of no fixed direction, and the hurricane in the Pacific Ocean will continue to move in a northwesterly or west-northwesterly direction. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in the city was 97.2, and the lowest was 78.0. On the same day last year, the highest was 93.2, and the lowest was 77.0.

Letter Received

To the Editor-in-Chief of Shen Bao, respectfully, I, the undersigned, having read your newspaper's local news section of the 19th of this month, which contained a section about the hotel owner Qilin raping a young girl named Amao, after reading it in detail, was deeply shocked. Upon investigation, the undersigned's name is Xi Lun, which is known in the neighbourhood, and is a legitimate businessman. Regarding this shameless act of rape, my conscience cannot allow it. The report published by your newspaper is not a factual account. The publication of this matter greatly affects the reputation of the undersigned. I request the Editor-in-Chief of your newspaper to immediately correct the record and publish it in the "Letters to the Editor" section. With gratitude, to the esteemed Editor-in-Chief of Shen Bao, Zhang Xi Lun, July 19, 1920

The Story of World Literature (183) by John Macy, Translated by Hu Zhongchi 187

Chapter Forty: The American Novel

During the latter half of his long career, the formal head of American literature, a friend and discerning mentor of Mark Twain, and a patron of promising young talent, was William Dean Howells. He was a delightful character, an artist to the fingertips, and a master of style from his first work to his last. To find a clumsy sentence in Howells would be as surprising as finding one in Flaubert or Anatole France. However, Howells was timid, lacking force. The "careful realism" he preached and practiced was a carefulness that was not an exquisite artistic restraint used by intelligence to subdue passion, because Howells had nothing to be careful about. Therefore, it was an empty carefulness. Of his many novels—for he was a diligent and extremely meticulous writer—three or four approached the realm of genius. "A Modern Instance," depicting the plight of ordinary little people suffering from petty troubles, was something entirely new in American novels. "The Rise of Silas Lapham" was probably the first novel with a common businessman as the protagonist. His later novel, "The Kentons," is one of his best works. In my opinion, even consistent admirers of Howells cannot fully appreciate its inherent value. He believed himself to be influenced by Tolstoy, but in his work, the traces of Tolstoy are no more evident than the influence of Fielding on Hawthorne. Howells was an admirable reader and wrote beautiful essays about books. Whether or not you agree with his opinions, you can always see a scholar with comprehensive knowledge in him.

America's greatest novelist, with the exception of birth, can hardly be said to be American. This is Henry James, who spent most of his mature life in Europe, and whose views were entirely European and worldly. He was one of the giants of 20th-century prose and an outstanding artist with only one important limitation. The so-called important limitation is that he had an incurable, but not despicable due to his extremely generous and sympathetic nature, snobbery. He was an intellectual "isolationist" with no knowledge of life except what could be learned in the reception rooms of grand hotels, art museums, and, needless to say, well-stocked libraries. Despite that limitation, he was a profound student of human character, in scientific terms, a psychologist. Many of the characters he portrayed were Americans in Europe, hence he was called the inventor of the international novel. However, a true international novelist should have played both sides and shown the Europeans in America as well. But Europeans in America were mostly laborers, while Americans in Europe were mostly idlers, and that was the class James knew. His works are divided into two periods. Belonging to the first period is the beautiful novel "Roderick Hudson," with a weak-willed American sculptor as the protagonist; the story of the pure and poignant ingenuous American girl who does not understand the complex morality and immorality of the ancient world, "Daisy Miller;" the somewhat pungent study of American brazenness and vitality and philistinism (the word "philistine" was a favorite of James, he used it so much that it became philistine itself) and a beautiful spiritual tragedy, "The Portrait of a Lady," with a truly tragic character as the protagonist, an uncomplicated but intelligent and honest person placed in an overly contrived situation; and "The American."

As James entered his second period, he became increasingly skillful and complex, pleasing his small group of devoted admirers and displeasing those who did not understand his technique. That technique was the complete objectification of characters. The people in the story move in very ordinary situations, or extremely difficult circumstances, in which one by one, their characteristics or traits flash out. If the reader reads the novel from beginning to end, then he will discover that the novelist has built a complete human character for himself. Two novels that illustrate that technique are "The Wings of the Dove" and "The Golden Bowl." James in his novels proceeds slowly and spends many pages to follow the development of a motive. However, he was also a master of the short story, and a volume containing eight to ten of his best short stories is entirely unrivaled in modern literature. He was also a sharp critic of French and English literature. Had he not turned to novels, he would have been ranked among the foremost writers of literary essays.

The story of a nation is not only narrated by rare talented writers, but also by many smaller writers, whose works, taken together, constitute that social history. America is necessarily divided into intellectual states. How can one know the farmer of Vermont and the farmer of Georgia? Two or three of those second-rate storytellers occupy a quasi-immortal place in the social record preserved by the art of the novel. The well-known poet T. B. Aldrich wrote several moving short stories, depicting not much of American life, but in which there is a graceful and humorous art. The same is true of Frank Stockton. His most famous short story is "The Lady, or the Tiger?" Southern life is expressed in the novels of several writers of true talent. Cable found romantic material in the old Creole and black life of New Orleans. That black slave is a prominently immortal figure in Harriet Beecher Stowe's "Uncle Tom's Cabin." The important figure of the Central West is preserved in Edward Eggleston's "The Hoosier School-Master," one of the first American novels to carefully study the dialect (so to speak, because it was published several years before "Huckleberry Finn"). The people and landscapes of New England are depicted for all time in the delicate stories of Mary Wilkins Freeman and Sarah Orne Jewett. I know of no other work by an American writer that is superior to Freeman's "The Revolt of Mother" in writing about ordinary people.

Market News 188

The Joint Savings Society of Jin Cheng, Zhong Nan, and Da Lu Banks has established a Western District branch at No. 1 Carter Road (intersection of Jing'an Temple Road and Carter Road). It opened yesterday (the 21st), and the depositors were extremely crowded. Most of the important figures in the local business community attended to offer their congratulations, making it a grand occasion. The amount of deposits received was also very enthusiastic, it is said.

The Shanghai Westside Paint Industry Association announced that the association's Standing Committee member Yin Runsheng, Executive Committee members Ding Fang'e, Tao Lianchun, Tao Zhongxiao, and more than ten others hosted Ma Shangjie and important staff members at the Du Yi Chu on Edward Road at 6:00 PM yesterday. During the banquet, Ma stood up and delivered a speech, roughly saying: "I am deeply grateful for the hospitality and grand banquet that you have shown me today. The association's affairs, from preparation to establishment, and from establishment to the present, have been deeply reliant on everyone's courage, enthusiasm, joint efforts, and concerted efforts to achieve satisfactory progress in gradually developing the common interests of the industry and gradually realizing them. I was previously nominated by everyone as one of the Standing Committee members, but I am deeply afraid that my shallow learning and limited experience will be insufficient to meet your expectations. The work and mission I bear must be based on the common interests of the association. Nothing else is to be considered. In the future, I deeply hope that everyone will work together to promote the association's affairs with unity and a genuine spirit." Next, Wang Shipeng stood up and gave a thank-you speech, roughly saying. During the banquet, everyone gathered together, and the clinking of glasses was quite a grand occasion for a time, it is said.

The United Machinery Factory on Route D'Ossi and Yangjia Dock Road announced that the factory has invented a new type of warp sizing machine, which is groundbreaking. This machine is flexible, precise, and ingenious. It can size both yarn and cloth. Its price is also low, and its output is especially fast. It can size 5,000 yards of warp yarn and cloth per day, which is most suitable for small-scale weaving factories. If this machine is available, imported single-yarn cloth will inevitably be rejected and eliminated on its own. The factory has scheduled a test run at 2:00 PM on July 22nd of the Gregorian calendar and sincerely invites people from all walks of life to come and visit. You are most welcome. The factory manufactures a wide variety of machines and has long been praised by the industrial and commercial communities, it is said.

Liang Chen Hao You She, located at the intersection of Beijing Road and Zhejiang Road, announced that it will be giving away 300,000 sample stationery envelopes starting today so that those who order printing can choose. Limit one per person. Must be stamped. Both in-person and mail requests are free. Each sample contains more than ten types of Chinese and Western paper materials, complete with regular, cursive, official, seal, running, Wei, and Song imitations, it is said.

The Da Ming Glasses Company on Tianjin Road announced that the company has invented domestically produced military goggles and telescopes, which are of good quality and low price, surpassing imported products. Dealers in the glasses, watches, and general merchandise industries in this city and other ports who wholesale from them are finding it difficult to keep up with demand, it is said.

Theater News 189

The Paris Grand Theater announced that starting today, it will screen the comedy "True and False Dukes" starring Betty Bronson and James Hall. The theme of the play is to awaken young women who are obsessed with vanity through satirical methods, and humorous twists and turns are interspersed to arouse the audience's interest, it is said.
